### [1] [SWE-Marathon: Can Agents Autonomously Complete Ultra-Long-Horizon Software Work?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07682v1)
*Rishi Desai,Jesse Hu,Joan Cabezas,Neel Harsola,Pratyush Shukla,Roey Ben Chaim,Adnan El Assadi,Omkaar Mukund Kamath,Fenil Faldu,Prannay Hebbar,Jiankai Sun,Yiyuan Li,Pramod Srinivasan,Ishan Gupta,Christopher Settles,Daniel Wang,Derek Chen,Pranav Raja,Albert Liu,Marek Šuppa,Nevasini Sasikumar,Luyang Kong,Erik Quintanilla,Xiangyi Li,Ivan Bercovich,Steven Dillmann*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: SWE-Marathon是一个包含20个长时任务的新基准，平均27.2M token，当前编码代理成功率低于30%，存在奖励黑客等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代理基准主要评估短时任务，不足以衡量代理在长时间工作流中的规划、长上下文理解和记忆能力，因此需要更长时间跨度的基准。

Method: 构建包含20个长时任务的SWE-Marathon基准，每个任务有可执行环境、人类参考答案和多层验证套件，并引入对抗性审查防止作弊。

Result: 当前前沿编码代理解决率低于30%，失败原因包括自我验证差、不可行报告和过早终止，13.8%轨迹出现奖励黑客行为。

Conclusion: SWE-Marathon揭示了当前代理在长时任务中的不足，为评估和推动代理能力提升提供了更具挑战性的基准。

中文摘要：人工智能代理越来越被期望完成需要持续数小时、数百万个token和复杂环境的长时工作流。然而，当前的代理基准主要评估短时任务，例如单个拉取请求、小工单或5-10分钟的练习，这限制了我们在规划、长上下文理解和记忆使用方面衡量代理能力的能力。我们引入了SWE-Marathon，这是一个包含20个跨软件工程及相关技术领域的长时任务的基准。每个任务包括一个独特的可执行环境、一个人类编写的参考答案以及一个多层验证套件。记录的代理尝试平均总token数为27.2M，使得SWE-Marathon在时间跨度上远长于现有的SWE和命令行代理基准。当前前沿编码代理解决的任务不到30%。失败通常源于自我验证差、自报告不可行和过早终止。我们还观察到13.8%的轨迹中存在奖励黑客行为，其中代理试图利用环境或验证器来绕过预期工作流。SWE-Marathon包括对测试套件和执行环境的对抗性审查，以及旨在防止捷径解决方案的多层检查。我们在https://swe-marathon.org/发布SWE-Marathon、评估代码和代理轨迹。

Original abstract: AI agents are increasingly expected to complete long-horizon workflows that require sustained progress over hours, millions of tokens, and complex environments. Yet current agent benchmarks largely evaluate short-form tasks, such as single pull requests, small tickets, or 5-10 minute exercises, limiting our ability to measure agents' capabilities in planning, long-context understanding, and memory use. We introduce SWE-Marathon, a benchmark of 20 long-horizon tasks spanning software engineering and adjacent technical domains. Each task consists of a unique executable environment, a human-written reference solution, and a multi-layer verification suite. Logged agent attempts average 27.2M total tokens, making SWE-Marathon substantially longer-horizon than existing SWE and command-line agent benchmarks. Current frontier coding agents solve fewer than 30% of tasks. Failures often arise from poor self-verification, self-reported infeasibility, and premature termination. We also observe reward-hacking behavior in 13.8% of rollouts, where agents attempt to exploit the environment or verifier to bypass the intended workflow. SWE-Marathon includes adversarial review of test suites and execution environments, as well as multi-layer checks designed to prevent shortcut solutions. We release SWE-Marathon, evaluation code, and agent trajectories at https://swe-marathon.org/.

</details>


### [2] [Review the Code, Not the Story: A Vision and Protocol for Code-First Peer Review](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07683v1)
*Jienan Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出以代码为先的同行评审框架，利用AI系统将评审焦点从手稿叙事转向可执行证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前以手稿为中心的评审流程使作者控制叙事，评审员难以验证实现细节和复现结果，导致无法有效检测无依据的主张。

Method: 提出代码优先的同行评审流程：作者提交可执行工件和主张清单，AI系统自动构建环境、执行实验、审计代码、映射证据并生成标准化评审包。

Result: 形式化了主张-证据合同，定义了评审视图和评审包抽象，给出了示例，并分析了AI偏见、注入攻击、模型稳定性等挑战。

Conclusion: AI作为评审基础设施可以转变同行评审的目标，但需要解决评估和治理挑战。

中文摘要：计算领域的同行评审仍然以作者撰写的稿件为中心，尽管许多主张的决定性证据存在于可执行代码、数据、配置和实验流程中。这种以稿件为先的工作流程赋予了作者对叙事框架的大量控制权，同时留给评审员有限的时间来检查实现细节、复现结果或检测无依据的主张。这篇愿景与协议论文提出了以代码为先的同行评审：作者提交可执行的研究工件和最少的主张清单；由会议控制的AI系统构建环境、执行实验、审计代码路径、将主张映射到证据，并生成标准化的评审包供人类评审员使用。目标不是取代评审员或为作者提供自动写作助手。相反，AI作为评审基础设施，将同行评审的目标从精心打磨的叙事转变为可执行的证据。我们形式化了主张-证据合同，定义了生成的评审视图和评审包抽象，给出了一个工作示例，概述了系统架构，并分析了评估和治理挑战，包括AI偏见、即时注入、模型不稳定性、可审计性和作者申诉。

Original abstract: Peer review in computational fields remains centered on author-written manuscripts, even though the decisive evidence for many claims resides in executable code, data, configurations, and experiment pipelines. This manuscript-first workflow gives authors substantial control over narrative framing while leaving reviewers with limited time to inspect implementation details, reproduce results, or detect unsupported claims. This vision and protocol paper proposes code-first peer review: authors submit executable research artifacts and minimal claim manifests; a venue-controlled AI system builds the environment, executes experiments, audits code paths, maps claims to evidence, and generates a standardized Review Package for human reviewers. The goal is not to replace reviewers or to give authors an automatic writing assistant. Instead, AI serves as review infrastructure that shifts the target of peer review from polished narratives to executable evidence. We formalize a claim-evidence contract, define the Generated Review View and Review Package abstractions, give a worked example, outline a system architecture, and analyze evaluation and governance challenges including AI bias, prompt injection, model instability, auditability, and author appeal.

</details>


### [3] [Chiseling Out Efficiency: Structured Skeleton Supervision for Efficient Code Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06821v1)
*Yu Yu,Zhihong Sun,Jia Li,Yao Wan,Chuanyi Li,Hongyu Zhang,Ruyun Wang,Tao Huang,Zhi Jin,Ge Li,Chen Lyu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出EffiSkel框架，通过显式提取和学习效率骨架（抽象结构模式），在多任务学习中联合优化代码生成和骨架预测，显著提升LLM生成代码的效率和功能正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法未能显式编码高效代码的结构模式，仅模仿完整优化方案，导致效率提升有限。

Method: 提出EffiSkel，利用三种互补策略提取效率骨架，并集成到多任务学习框架中联合优化代码生成和骨架预测。

Result: 在Mercury上，使用DeepSeek-Coder (7B)时，ER比EffiCoder高11.11%，比CodeDPO高3.71%；AS分别高0.36和0.22。

Conclusion: 显式建模效率骨架能有效提高LLM生成代码的运行时性能。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）能够生成语法正确且功能完整的程序，极大地简化了软件开发。然而，近期研究表明，这些程序通常比人类优化的对应版本运行得慢得多。现有弥补这一效率差距的方法通常涉及在生成后迭代优化代码或在高效代码语料库上微调模型。然而，这些方法仅通过模仿完整的优化解决方案将效率信号暴露给模型，而没有明确编码实现高运行时性能所必需的结构性代码模式。解决这一差距存在两个核心挑战：（1）提取和表示嵌入在复杂语法和控制流中的潜在效率导向的结构模式，（2）在不破坏LLM语义训练稳定性的情况下有效学习这些模式。为应对这些挑战，我们提出EffiSkel，一种效率骨架引导框架，通过利用三种互补策略明确提取和学习效率骨架——支撑高效代码的抽象、可重用的结构模式。这些骨架被集成到一个多任务学习框架中，该框架联合优化代码生成和骨架预测。跨多种编程语言和基准的实验表明，EffiSkel显著增强了功能正确性和效率，在Mercury上使用DeepSeek-Coder（7B）时，效率比（ER）相比EffiCoder提高了+11.11%，相比CodeDPO提高了+3.71%，平均加速比（AS）相比EffiCoder提高了+0.36，相比CodeDPO提高了+0.22。这些结果凸显了显式建模效率骨架在提高LLM生成代码运行时性能方面的有效性。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are capable of generating syntactically correct and functionally complete programs, greatly streamlining software development. However, recent studies reveal that these programs typically execute substantially slower than human-optimized counterparts. Existing approaches to bridging this efficiency gap typically involve either iteratively optimizing code after generation or fine-tuning models on corpora of efficient code. Yet, these methods expose the model to efficiency signals only by mimicking complete, optimized solutions, without explicitly encoding the structural code patterns essential for achieving high runtime performance. Addressing this gap presents two core challenges: (1) extracting and representing latent, efficiency-oriented structural patterns embedded within complex syntax and control flows, and (2) effectively learning these patterns without destabilizing the semantic training of LLMs. To tackle these challenges, we propose EffiSkel, an efficiency skeleton-guided framework that explicitly extracts and learns efficiency skeletons-abstract, reusable structural patterns underpinning efficient code-by leveraging three complementary strategies. These skeletons are integrated into a multi-task learning regime that jointly optimizes code generation and skeleton prediction. Experiments across multiple programming languages and benchmarks demonstrate that EffiSkel significantly enhances both functional correctness and efficiency, resulting on Mercury with DeepSeek-Coder (7B) a +11.11% (vs. EffiCoder) and +3.71% (vs. CodeDPO) higher Efficiency Ratio (ER), and a +0.36 (vs. EffiCoder) and +0.22 (vs. CodeDPO) increase in Average Speedup (AS). These results highlight the effectiveness of explicitly modeling efficiency skeletons in improving the runtime performance of code generated by LLMs.

</details>


### [4] [SkelDPO: A Skeleton-Guided Direct Preference Optimization Framework for Efficient Code Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06826v1)
*Yu Yu,Chen Lyu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出SkelDPO框架，通过骨架引导的偏好优化提升代码生成效率，在多项指标上超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Code LLMs虽能生成语义正确代码，但未显式建模影响效率的结构因素，无法学习高效实现的细粒度骨架特征。

Method: SkelDPO：从数据集中识别高效/低效实现，通过比较定位效率关键点；引入联合代码和骨架偏好损失进行训练，同时学习语义正确性和效率结构。

Result: 在Pass@1、Beyond@1、Effi@1上分别比SOTA提升3-6%、3-7%、2-5%，复杂任务提升更显著。

Conclusion: SkelDPO提供了骨架级效率对齐的新视角，打破了传统偏好优化依赖正确性或效率对的局限，有效提升代码生成效率。

中文摘要：随着代码大型语言模型（Code LLMs）在语义正确性方面取得显著进展，执行效率已成为评估其实用性的越来越重要的维度。然而，现有方法通常将完整程序作为训练期间的单一优化目标，而没有显式建模影响效率的结构因素。因此，尽管这些模型能够生成语义正确的代码，但它们无法在细粒度层面上学习导致高效实现的底层骨架特征。为了解决这一局限性，我们提出了SkelDPO（骨架引导的直接偏好优化），一种骨架引导的偏好优化框架，系统地提升代码生成的效率。SkelDPO首先从代码数据集中识别高效和低效的实现，并通过比较分析定位它们的效率倾向点和低效倾向点，形成高效骨架与低效骨架之间的对齐信号。在训练过程中，引入了联合代码和骨架偏好损失，使模型在学习语义正确性的同时，强化其对代码中效率关键组件的理解。结果表明，SkelDPO持续超越现有方法：与仅依赖高效和低效代码偏好优化的SOTA方法相比，它在Pass@1、Beyond@1和Effi@1上分别提升了3-6%、3-7%和2-5%，在复杂任务上提升更为显著。总体而言，SkelDPO为骨架级效率对齐提供了新视角，突破了传统偏好优化仅依赖正确性或效率对的限制。所有数据集和源代码已在https://github.com/icpcSkelDPO/SkelDPO公开提供。

Original abstract: With the remarkable progress of Code Large Language Models (Code LLMs) in achieving semantic correctness, execution efficiency has become an increasingly important dimension for evaluating their practical utility. However, existing approaches typically treat full programs as a single optimization target during training, without explicitly modeling the structural factors that influence efficiency. As a result, although these models can generate semantically correct code, they fail to learn, at a fine-grained level, the underlying skeleton features that lead to efficient implementations. To address this limitation, we propose SkelDPO (Skeleton-Guided Direct Preference Optimization), a skeleton-guided preference optimization framework that systematically enhances the efficiency of code generation. SkelDPO first identifies efficient and inefficient implementations from the code dataset and, through comparative analysis, locates their efficiency-prone and inefficiency-prone points, forming alignment signals between efficiency and inefficiency skeletons. During training, a joint code and skeleton preference loss is introduced, enabling the model to learn semantic correctness while reinforcing its understanding of efficiency-critical components in code. Results show that SkelDPO consistently surpasses existing methods: compared with SOTA method that relies solely on efficient and inefficient code preference optimization, it improves Pass@1, Beyond@1, and Effi@1 by 3-6%, 3-7%, and 2-5%, with greater improvements observed on complex tasks. Overall, SkelDPO provides a new perspective on skeleton-level efficiency alignment, breaking the limitation of conventional preference optimization that relies solely on correctness or efficiency pairs. All datasets and source code are publicly available at: https://github.com/icpcSkelDPO/SkelDPO.

</details>


### [5] [LLM Agent-Assisted Reverse Engineering with Quantitative Readability Metrics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06838v1)
*Neil Archibald,Ruben Thijssen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出QRS框架，结合结构相似性门控和三个可读性子指标，引导LLM代理在不牺牲正确性的前提下提升反编译代码的可读性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动反编译器生成的C代码可读性差，现有方法缺乏定量指导，导致改进不一致或牺牲可读性。

Method: 通过三阶段研究演进，提出QRS框架，包含结构相似性门控和三个子指标（词汇意外性、结构简单性、惯用质量），并用该指标引导LLM代理进行代码改进。

Result: QRS引导的改进使LLM代理能够做出有针对性的可读性提升，同时保持代码正确性。

Conclusion: QRS框架有效指导LLM代理提升反编译代码可读性，作为更广泛逆向工程工作流程的背景。

中文摘要：自动反编译器生成功能正确但通常难以阅读的C代码。本文针对逆向工程工作流程中的一个阶段：使用由定量指标引导的LLM代理来提高反编译代码的可读性。我们提出了一个三阶段的研究演进。第一阶段（通过Ghidra MCP的工具驱动引导）由于缺乏定量指导而导致覆盖不完全和改进不一致。第二阶段（仅使用结构相似性验证）揭示了代理以非预期的方式优化指标，生成结构等价但可读性更差的代码。我们的贡献是定量可读性评分（QRS）框架，这是一个组合指标，结合了结构相似性门控和三个独立可读性子指标（词汇意外性、结构简单性和惯用质量）。我们展示了QRS引导的改进使LLM代理能够在不牺牲正确性的情况下进行有针对性的可读性改进。我们提供了更广泛的逆向工程工作流程（二进制提升、反编译清理和实现功能等价）的讨论作为背景，然而，这超出了范围。

Original abstract: Automatic decompilers produce functionally correct but often unreadable C code. This paper addresses one stage of the reverse engineering workflow: improving the readability of decompiled code using LLM agents guided by quantitative metrics.
  We present a three-phase research evolution. Phase 1 (tool-driven steering via Ghidra MCP) suffered from incomplete coverage and inconsistent improvements due to lack of quantitative guidance. Phase 2 (structural similarity validation alone) revealed that agents optimize for metrics in unintended ways, producing structurally equivalent but less readable code. Our contribution is the Quantitative Readability Score (QRS) framework, a composite metric combining a structural similarity gate with three independent readability sub-metrics (Lexical Surprisal, Structural Simplicity, and Idiomatic Quality).
  We demonstrate that QRS-guided refinement enables LLM agents to make targeted readability improvements without sacrificing correctness. We provide a discussion of the broader reverse engineering workflow (binary lifting, decompilation cleanup, and achieving functional equivalence) as context, however, it remains out of scope.

</details>


### [6] [Empirical Study on the Characteristics and Evolution of AI-usage in GitHub Repositories: Evidence from Code Comments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06843v1)
*Abdullah Al Mujahid,Preetha Chatterjee,Mia Mohammad Imran*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过分析GitHub上的AI引用评论和代码，发现开发者主要用LLM进行代码实现，后续提交中人类持续监督和调整AI生成的代码，且AI使用逐渐从代码生成转向知识支持和代码增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究多孤立评估LLM输出，缺乏对开发者如何在真实项目中调整AI工具的实际考察。

Method: 分析了35,361条GitHub代码评论及关联代码块，通过开放编码500条样本建立分类法，使用两个LLM分类器标注全数据集并用Dawid-Skene聚合，同时分析12,996条后续提交信息及时间趋势（2022年12月至2026年3月）。

Result: 开发者主要用LLM进行代码实现、增强、调试、文档和测试；后续提交频繁出现重构清理、功能集成扩展和错误修复，表明人类持续监督；时间趋势显示评论从直接代码生成转向知识支持和代码增强。

Conclusion: AI工具不仅作为代码生成辅助，还作为协作支持机制嵌入开发，其输出需经开发者持续改进、扩展和纠正。

中文摘要：开发者越来越多地在日常软件工作流程中使用诸如ChatGPT、Copilot和Claude等AI工具，但先前的研究通常孤立地评估LLM输出，而不是检查开发者如何在真实项目中调整它们。我们分析了35,361条明确提及AI使用的GitHub代码评论及其关联的代码块。我们首先对500条独特的评论和代码块进行开放编码，以推导出AI辅助开发活动的分类法，然后使用两个基于LLM的分类器注释整个数据集，并通过Dawid-Skene期望最大化聚合预测。我们还分析了12,996条后续提交信息，以研究AI辅助代码在引入后的演变，并检查了从2022年12月到2026年3月的时间趋势。我们的结果表明，开发者主要将LLM用于代码实现，其次是代码增强、调试、文档编写和测试。后续提交经常涉及重构和清理、功能集成和扩展以及错误修复，表明在调整AI辅助代码时存在持续的人类监督。随着时间的推移，提及AI的评论从直接的代码生成转向知识和概念支持以及代码增强。这些发现表明，AI工具不仅作为代码生成辅助工具，而且作为协作支持机制嵌入到开发过程中，其输出由开发者随时间不断改进、扩展和纠正。

Original abstract: Developers increasingly use AI tools such as ChatGPT, Copilot, and Claude in everyday software workflows, but prior studies often evaluate LLM outputs in isolation rather than examining how developers adapt them in real projects. We analyze 35,361 GitHub code comments that explicitly reference AI use and their associated code blocks. We first open-code 500 unique comments and code blocks to derive a taxonomy of AI-assisted development activities, then annotate the full dataset using two LLM-based classifiers and aggregate predictions with Dawid-Skene expectation-maximization. We also analyze 12,996 subsequent commit messages to study how AI-assisted code evolves after introduction, and examine temporal trends from December 2022 to March 2026. Our results show that developers primarily use LLMs for code implementation, followed by code enhancement, debugging, documentation, and testing. Subsequent commits frequently involve refactoring and cleanup, feature integration and extension, and bug fixing, indicating sustained human oversight in adapting AI-assisted code. Over time, AI-referencing comments shift from direct code generation toward knowledge and conceptual support and code enhancement. These findings suggest that AI tools are becoming embedded not only as code-generation aids, but also as collaborative support mechanisms whose outputs are refined, extended, and corrected by developers over time.

### [7] [From Custom Logic to APIs: Understanding and Recommending API Replacement Refactorings](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06912v1)
*Bridget Nyirongo,Yanjie Jiang,Yuxia Zhang,Hui Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 首次对API替换重构进行实证研究，提出AKIRA混合框架，在推荐召回率和精确率上显著超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有重构工具依赖预定义模板，难以检测复杂的多语句语义等价API替换重构机会，导致支持有限。

Method: 对166,299次提交进行实证研究，提出AKIRA框架，结合模式确定性启发式和重构感知知识库。

Result: 在内置数据集上召回率90%、精确率88%；在RETIWA数据集上召回率从21%提升至81%，精确率从40%提升至78%。

Conclusion: 结合静态模式匹配与语义推理可有效支持复杂API替换重构的自动化推荐。

中文摘要：软件重构对于维护代码质量至关重要。然而，API替换重构（用API调用替换自定义逻辑）仍未得到充分探索。现有重构工具对检测此类机会的支持有限，因为它们依赖于预定义的模板，难以捕获复杂的多语句语义等价物。为解决这一限制，我们通过对六个开源Java项目的166,299次提交进行挖掘，并对精心筛选的1,800次提交进行手动分析，识别出366个经过验证的实例，从而对API替换重构进行了首次实证研究，以描述其范围、类别和重复模式。基于这些洞察，我们提出了AKIRA（自适应知识发现与检索），一个混合框架，将模式确定性启发式方法与重构感知知识库相结合，以评估推荐API替换重构的实际可行性。我们的评估显示，AKIRA在手动策划的数据集上实现了90%的召回率和88%的精确率。此外，在外部的RETIWA数据集上，AKIRA显著提升了现有技术水平，将召回率从21%提高到81%，精确率从40%提高到78%。这些结果证明了结合静态模式匹配与语义推理来支持复杂API替换重构自动推荐的有效性。

Original abstract: Software refactoring is essential for maintaining code quality. However, API replacement refactoring, which replaces custom logic with API calls, remains underexplored. Existing refactoring tools provide limited support for detecting such opportunities because they rely on predefined templates and have difficulty capturing complex, multi-statement semantic equivalents. To address this limitation, we conduct the first empirical study of API replacement refactorings by mining 166,299 commits across six open-source Java projects and manually analyzing a curated subset of 1,800 commits, from which we identify 366 validated instances to characterize their scope, categories, and recurring patterns. Based on these insights, we propose AKIRA (Adaptive Knowledge Discovery and Retrieval), a hybrid framework that integrates pattern-deterministic heuristics with a refactoring-aware knowledge base to assess the practical feasibility of recommending API replacement refactorings. Our evaluation shows that AKIRA achieves 90% recall and 88% precision on a manually curated dataset. Furthermore, on the external RETIWA dataset, AKIRA significantly improves the state of the art by increasing recall from 21% to 81% and precision from 40% to 78%. These results demonstrate the effectiveness of combining static pattern matching with semantic reasoning to support the automation of recommending complex API replacement refactorings.

### [8] [Porting Declarative UI to HarmonyOS: A Heuristic-guided LLM Approach](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07085v1)
*Kunwu Zheng,Pengyu Xue,Zhen Yang,Xiran Lyu,Peishi Lai,Mengying Zhao,Yutian Tang,Huizhi Zhang,Xianhang Li,Linhao Wu,Chengyi Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出 ArkTrans 方法，通过启发式构建骨架和模式匹配后修复，结合 LLM，实现从 Android/iOS 到 HarmonyOS ArkUI 的自动 UI 转换，达到 90.67% 的编译成功率和高视觉保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HarmonyOS 需要从 Android 和 iOS 迁移软件，UI 转换是关键环节，但现有方法针对后端逻辑或传统命令式 UI，不适用于最新的声明式范式（如 KJC、SwiftUI 和 ArkUI），因此需要新的自动翻译方法。

Method: 提出 ArkTrans，包含两个模块：1) 启发式构建 ArkUI 骨架：从源 PL 提取元数据以指导 LLM 初始翻译；2) 基于模式匹配的后修复：执行经验性规则修复剩余语法错误。

Result: 构建 100 样本基准（KJC/SwiftUI 到 ArkUI），直接 LLM 无法编译任何页面，而 ArkTrans 最多 90.67% 的文件可成功编译，且视觉保真度高。

Conclusion: ArkTrans 能有效解决声明式 UI 跨平台翻译中的语言不熟悉和语法混乱问题，显著提升编译成功率和视觉保真度，为 HarmonyOS 软件迁移提供了可行方案。

中文摘要：作为一个新兴的操作系统，HarmonyOS 对从 Android 和 iOS 等平台进行软件迁移有重大需求，其中用户界面（UI）的转换是一个关键环节。然而，最新的 UI 开发已转向声明式范式，例如用于 Android 的 Kotlin Jetpack Compose (KJC)、用于 iOS 的 SwiftUI 和用于 HarmonyOS 的 ArkUI，这使得先前的转换方法不再适用，因为它们要么针对后端逻辑，要么针对传统的命令式 UI。因此，本文以 ArkUI 为目标，提出了一种自动转换方法，名为 ArkTrans，用于将 UI 文件从 Android 和 iOS 迁移到 HarmonyOS。ArkTrans 克服了转换过程中的两个显著挑战：(1) 编程语言（PL）不熟悉，以及 (2) 严重的语法混乱。针对第一个挑战，ArkTrans 通过从源 PL 提取元数据来启发式地构建 ArkUI 骨架，从而指导大型语言模型（LLMs）的初始转换。针对第二个挑战，ArkTrans 通过模式匹配执行经验性揭示的后修复规则，以修复大部分剩余的语法错误。为了检验 ArkTrans 的有效性，我们构建了一个从 KJC/SwiftUI 到 ArkUI 的 100 样本并行 UI 页面转换基准，在文件级别进行。大量实验表明，使用直接/一次提示的 LLMs 无法转换任何可编译的 UI 页面。相比之下，最多有 90.67% 的 ArkTrans 转换文件能够成功编译，并具有高度的视觉保真度。

Original abstract: As an emerging operating system, HarmonyOS has a significant demand for software migration from platforms such as Android and iOS, where the User Interface (UI) translation accounts for a critical link. However, the latest UI development has shifted to declarative paradigms, e.g., Kotlin Jetpack Compose (KJC) for Android, SwiftUI for iOS, and ArkUI for HarmonyOS, rendering prior translation approaches inapplicable, as they target either backend logic or legacy imperative UIs.
  As such, this paper targets ArkUI and proposes an automatic translation approach, namely ArkTrans, to port UI files from Android and iOS to HarmonyOS.
  ArkTrans overcomes two salient challenges during the translation: (1) Programming Language (PL) unfamiliarity, and (2) severe syntactic chaos. Towards the first challenge, ArkTrans heuristically constructs ArkUI skeletons by extracting metadata from source PL, thereby guiding LLMs' initial translation. As for the second challenge, ArkTrans executes empirically revealed post-fixing rules via pattern matching to repair most of the remaining syntactic errors. To examine the effectiveness of ArkTrans, we construct a 100-sample parallel UI page translation benchmark from KJC/SwiftUI to ArkUI at the file level. Extensive experiments demonstrate that LLMs with direct/one-shot prompting cannot translate a single compilable UI page. In contrast, at most 90.67\% ArkTrans-translated files can be successfully compiled with high visual fidelity.

### [9] [MetaConfigurator: AI-Assisted RDF Authoring from JSON Data](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07094v2)
*Felix Neubauer,Mahdi Jafarkhani,Kenichi Endo,Jürgen Pleiss,Benjamin Uekermann*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出一个集成AI辅助的RDF创作视图，实现从JSON等数据到RDF的转换、查询和可视化，并基于MOF合成实验验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JSON数据缺乏语义互操作性，现有工具难以进行一致解释和链接数据集成。

Method: 扩展JSON Schema编辑器MetaConfigurator，集成RML映射、SPARQL查询、知识图谱可视化等，并利用AI辅助IRI自动完成和SPARQL生成。

Result: 能够将实验室数据（如MOF合成协议）转换为基于本体的JSON-LD，并支持交互式查询和探索知识图谱。

Conclusion: 该集成环境降低了语义Web技术的使用门槛，保留了实验背景，实现了传统数据管理与语义Web的无缝桥接。

中文摘要：科学工作流越来越多地生成结构化的JSON数据，这些数据易于交换，但由于缺乏语义互操作性，难以在不同系统间一致地解释。虽然JSON Schema确保了结构验证，但它不原生支持链接数据语义。本文介绍了一个RDF创作视图，扩展了开源JSON Schema编辑器MetaConfigurator，使研究人员能够使用AI辅助的RML映射将现有的JSON、YAML或CSV数据转换为RDF，细化三元组，执行SPARQL查询，可视化知识图谱，并在单个集成的Web界面中导出RDF序列化。此工作流由本体感知的IRI自动完成、JSON-LD文本视图与RDF三元组表之间的双向同步以及基于自然语言提示的AI辅助SPARQL查询生成提供支持。我们使用金属有机框架（MOF）合成实验的实验室数据演示了该工作流。协议数据描述试剂、步骤和数量，通过RML映射从JSON转换为基于本体的JSON-LD。然后我们细化语义表示，查询实验条件与结果之间的关系，并交互式地探索生成的知识图谱。这种集成环境将传统的结构化数据管理与语义Web技术桥接起来，同时通过AI辅助保留实验背景并降低技术门槛。

Original abstract: Scientific workflows increasingly generate structured JSON data that is easy to exchange but difficult to interpret consistently across systems due to lacking semantic interoperability. While JSON Schema ensures structural validation, it provides no native support for Linked Data semantics.
  This paper presents an RDF Authoring View extending the open-source JSON Schema editor MetaConfigurator, enabling researchers to transform existing JSON, YAML, or CSV data into RDF using AI-assisted RML mappings, refine triples, execute SPARQL queries, visualize knowledge graphs, and export RDF serializations within a single integrated web interface. This workflow is supported by ontology-aware IRI auto-completion, bidirectional synchronization between JSON-LD text views and RDF triple tables, and AI-assisted SPARQL query generation from natural language hints.
  We demonstrate the workflow using laboratory data from metal-organic framework (MOF) synthesis experiments. Protocol data describing reagents, procedure steps, and quantities is converted from JSON to ontology-based JSON-LD via RML mappings. We then refine the semantic representation, query relationships between experimental conditions and outcomes, and explore the resulting knowledge graph interactively. This integrated environment bridges conventional structured data management with Semantic Web technologies while preserving experimental context and lowering technical barriers through AI assistance.

### [10] [Are We Lost in the Woods? Detecting Silent Semantic Faults for Random Forest Classifiers with Data-informed Static Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07709v1)
*Willem Meijer,Louis Ohl,Kristian Sandahl,Daniel Varro*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出数据驱动的静态分析技术，通过提取ML流水线为DAG并评估API契约，检测随机森林脚本中的静默语义错误，实现91%精度和亚秒级开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ML中的静默语义错误（如不平衡数据集）通常需要昂贵训练后才能发现，造成资源浪费，亟需早期检测方法。

Method: 将ML脚本提取为有向无环图（DAG），并基于形式化API契约分析结构、数据和超参数错误，利用聚合数据属性实现无需实际数据集的分析。

Result: 在真实Kaggle笔记本上达到91%精度和亚秒级运行时开销，发现12%-18%的笔记本存在静默语义错误。

Conclusion: 数据驱动的静态分析能有效检测ML静默语义错误，适合集成到开发流程，减少调试负担。

中文摘要：虽然机器学习软件需要有效的质量保证，但机器学习工程师仍然会遇到静默语义错误，例如不平衡数据集，这些问题会降低预测性能而没有明显症状。这些错误通常是在昂贵的训练周期之后才被检测到，导致大量资源浪费。我们提出了一种数据驱动的静态分析技术，用于检测使用流行随机森林分类器的机器学习脚本中的静默语义错误。我们的方法将机器学习流水线提取为有向无环图，并根据形式化的API契约对其进行评估，以检测结构、数据和超参数错误。我们的分析使用聚合的数据属性，即使由于保密限制而无法访问数据集，也能检测错误。我们将该技术实现为一个开源工具dille，并在使用随机森林分类器的真实Kaggle笔记本上进行了评估。结果表明，该工具能够以91%的精度和亚秒级运行时开销识别相关的语义错误，使其适合集成到集成开发环境、智能工作流和持续集成流水线中。我们的实证研究表明，使用随机森林分类器的现有机器学习笔记本中有12%到18%受到静默语义错误的影响，这突显了数据驱动静态分析在减轻机器学习调试负担方面的直接实用价值。

Original abstract: While machine learning (ML) software necessitates effective quality assurance, ML engineers still encounter silent semantic faults, such as imbalanced datasets, that degrade prediction performance without apparent symptoms. These faults are typically detected after expensive training cycles, causing significant resource waste. We propose a data-informed static analysis technique to detect silent semantic faults in ML scripts that use the popular random forest classifier. Our approach extracts ML pipelines into directed acyclic graphs and evaluates them against formalized API contracts to detect structural, data, and hyperparameter faults. Our analysis uses aggregated data properties, enabling fault detection even when datasets are inaccessible due to confidentiality restrictions. We implemented this technique in an open-source tool, dille, and evaluated it on real-world Kaggle notebooks that use the random forest classifier. Our results demonstrate that the tool identifies relevant semantic faults with 91% precision and sub-second runtime overhead, making it suitable for integration into integrated development environments, agentic workflows, and continuous integration pipelines. Our empirical study reveals that 12% to 18% of existing ML notebooks that use the random forest classifier are affected by silent semantic faults, highlighting the immediate practical utility of data-informed static analysis in reducing the burden of ML debugging.

### [11] [SWE-Explore: Benchmarking How Coding Agents Explore Repositories](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07297v1)
*Shaoqiu Zhang,Yuhang Wang,Jialiang Liang,Yuling Shi,Wenhao Zeng,Maoquan Wang,Shilin He,Ningyuan Xu,Siyu Ye,Kai Cai,Xiaodong Gu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了SWE-Explore基准，专门评估编码代理的仓库探索能力，通过行级标注和覆盖/排序/效率指标，发现代理式探索者优于传统检索方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有仓库级编码基准（如SWE-bench）仅将任务视为整体成功与否，忽略了细粒度能力（如仓库理解、代码定位等），因此需要一个专门评估探索能力的基准。

Method: 创建SWE-Explore基准，包含848个问题与203个仓库，从成功代理轨迹中提取行级真实代码区域，要求探索者在固定行预算内返回排序后的相关区域，并从覆盖、排序、上下文效率三方面评估。

Result: 代理式探索者（如编码代理）在探索任务上明显优于经典检索方法；文件级定位已较强，但行级覆盖与高效排序仍是区分先进探索者的关键。

Conclusion: SWE-Explore有效评估了编码代理的仓库探索能力，揭示了行级覆盖率与排序效率的重要性，为未来代理设计提供了方向。

中文摘要：诸如SWE-bench等仓库级编码基准测试推动了编码代理能力的迅速提升。然而，这些基准测试通常将编码任务视为一个整体的二元预测问题（例如，已解决或未解决），忽略了代理的细粒度能力，如仓库理解、上下文检索、代码定位和错误诊断。在本文中，我们引入了SWE-Explore，这是一个专门评估编码代理仓库探索能力（一项关键能力）的基准测试。给定一个仓库和一个问题，SWE-Explore要求探索者在固定的行预算内返回一个相关代码区域的排序列表。SWE-Explore涵盖了848个问题，涉及10种编程语言和203个开源仓库。对于每个实例，我们从成功解决同一问题的独立代理轨迹中提取行级真实情况，提炼出它们的解决路径实际参考的具体代码区域。我们从覆盖率、排序和上下文效率维度评估探索能力，表明这些指标与下游修复行为密切相关。在广泛的检索方法、通用编码代理和专用定位器中，我们发现代理式探索者明显优于经典检索方法。虽然对于现代方法来说，文件级定位已经很强，但行级覆盖率和高效排序仍然是区分最先进探索者的关键轴。

Original abstract: Repository-level coding benchmarks such as SWE-bench have driven a rapid surge in the capabilities of coding agents. Yet they usually treat coding tasks as a holistic, binary prediction problem (e.g., resolved or unresolved), neglecting fine-grained agent capabilities such as repository understanding, context retrieval, code localization, and bug diagnosis. In this paper, we introduce SWE-Explore, a benchmark that isolates the evaluation of repository exploration, a critical capability of coding agents. Given a repository and an issue, SWE-Explore asks an explorer to return a ranked list of relevant code regions under a fixed line budget. SWE-Explore covers 848 issues across 10 programming languages and 203 open-source repositories. For each instance, we derive line-level ground truth from independent agent trajectories that successfully solved the same issue, distilling the specific code regions their solution paths actually consulted. We evaluate exploration along coverage, ranking, and context-efficiency dimensions, showing that these metrics strongly track downstream repair behavior. Across a broad set of retrieval methods, general coding agents, and specialized localizers, we find that agentic explorers form a clear tier above classical retrieval. While file-level localization is already strong for modern methods, line-level coverage and efficient ranking remain the key axes differentiating state-of-the-art explorers.

</details>


### [12] [QBugLM: An Agentic Benchmarking Framework for LLM-based Quantum Software Debugging](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07314v1)
*An B. B. Pham,Hoa T. Nguyen,Muhammad Usman*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出QBugLM多智能体框架用于自动化量子软件调试，通过迭代反馈显著提升修复成功率，并发现简单结构化提示在固定资源下优于复杂推理策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子软件错误常表现为非显式错误，传统方法难以检测和修复，而LLM在量子代码调试方面的能力尚未被充分探索。

Method: 提出QBugLM多智能体框架，包含分类驱动的错误注入、LLM检测与修复、仿真验证，并在OpenQASM 3.0程序上评估不同LLM和提示策略。

Result: 单次迭代反馈使Pass@1从低于25%升至超过80%；简单结构化提示在固定资源下优于Chain-of-Thought和ReAct。

Conclusion: 工作为基准测试LLM调试量子程序能力迈出第一步，提供自动修复的实用见解。

中文摘要：量子软件的错误常常表现为无声的、不正确的输出，而非显式错误，这使得传统技术难以检测和修复。尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在经典软件工程任务中表现出色，但它们调试量子代码的能力仍 largely unexplored。为弥补这一差距，我们提出 QBugLM，一个多智能体框架，该框架自动化了量子软件调试流程，从基于分类法的错误注入，到基于 LLM 的检测和修复，最后到基于模拟的验证，适用于框架无关的 OpenQASM 3.0 程序。我们进一步使用 QBugLM 进行综合案例研究，以评估两个 LLM（Claude 4.6 Sonnet 和 Qwen3 Coder Next）在不同提示策略、错误类别和量子程序下的表现。我们的结果表明，迭代反馈至关重要，单次重试使 Pass@1 从低于 25% 提升至超过 80%。此外，在固定资源约束下，对于具备推理能力的模型，更简单的结构化提示甚至可以超越 Chain-of-Thought 和 ReAct。我们的工作朝着基准测试 LLM 调试量子程序的能力迈出了初步步伐，并为未来自动化量子软件修复的努力提供了实用见解。

Original abstract: Quantum software bugs often yield silent, incorrect outputs rather than explicit errors, making them particularly difficult to detect and repair with conventional techniques. Although large language models (LLMs) have shown strong performance on classical software engineering tasks, their ability to debug quantum code remains largely unexplored. To bridge this gap, we propose QBugLM, a multi-agent framework that automates the quantum software debugging pipeline, from taxonomy-driven bug injection to LLM-based detection and repair, and finally to simulation-based validation, for framework-agnostic OpenQASM 3.0 programs. We further conduct a comprehensive case study using QBugLM to benchmark two LLMs, Claude 4.6 Sonnet and Qwen3 Coder Next, across different prompting strategies, bug categories, and quantum programs. Our results show that iterative feedback is critical, as a single retry raises Pass@1 from below 25% to above 80%. Moreover, simpler structured prompting can even outperform Chain-of-Thought and ReAct for reasoning-capable models under fixed-resource constraints. Our work takes initial steps toward benchmarking LLM capabilities for debugging quantum programs and offers practical insights to support future efforts in automated quantum software repair.

</details>


### [13] [Is US Defense Acquisition Ready to Acquire AI-Enabled Capabilities? Assessing the DoD Software Acquisition Pathway Through a Scenario-Based Policy Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07393v1)
*Daniel Lugo,James C. Davis*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文评估了美国国防部软件采购路径（SWP）对AI采购的适用性，发现核心指南缺乏可操作性，AI特定控制分散，建议增加子路径和改进工件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估现有软件采购路径（SWP）是否足以应对AI系统对动态数据、演变模型和治理的独特需求，以弥合政策与实践之间的差距。

Method: 基于场景的评估，使用政策场景分析（Policy Scenario Analysis），通过追踪一个假设的AI赋能项目在SWP关键规划活动中的流程，分析政策如何转化为项目工件和决策。

Result: 治理堆栈为迭代交付和AI测试提供了可行基础，但核心指南存在可操作性问题：AI特定控制（数据来源、生命周期管理、人类监督）分散在补充文件中，未嵌入执行机制，导致项目办公室依赖不一致的局部解释。

Conclusion: 建议增加一个AI支持子路径并进行有针对性的工件改进，以更好地弥合政策与工件之间的差距，提升AI采购的可操作性。

中文摘要：随着AI系统从实验原型过渡到关键任务工具，它们对动态数据、不断发展的模型和治理的依赖引发了关于现有采购途径能否跟上的问题。美国国防部通过适应性采购框架对其采购流程进行了现代化改造，其中软件采购路径（SWP）是采购软件密集型能力的主要机制。本文评估了SWP是否足以应对AI采购的独特需求。在这项工作中，我们进行了一项基于场景的评估，追踪一个假设的AI赋能项目通过关键的SWP规划活动，以评估政策如何转化为项目工件和决策。我们使用政策场景分析来检查以SWP为中心的治理堆栈是否为AI采购提供了足够的可操作支持。治理堆栈为迭代交付和AI测试提供了可行基础。然而，我们在核心指南中发现了一个反复出现的可操作性问题。针对数据来源、生命周期管理和人类监督的AI特定控制措施仍然分布在补充文件中，而不是嵌入到执行SWP的项目面对机制中。这种脱节使得项目办公室依赖于不一致的地方解释。最后，我们建议增加一个AI支持子路径和有针对性的人工制品改进，以更好地弥合政策与人工制品之间的差距。

Original abstract: As AI systems transition from experimental prototypes to mission-critical tools, their dependence on dynamic data, evolving models, and governance raises questions about whether existing acquisition pathways can keep pace. The U.S. Department of Defense has modernized its acquisition processes through the Adaptive Acquisition Framework, with the Software Acquisition Pathway (SWP) serving as the primary mechanism for acquiring software-intensive capabilities. This paper evaluates whether SWP is sufficient to address the unique demands of AI acquisition.
  In this work, we perform a scenario-based evaluation that traces a notional AI-enabled program through key SWP planning activities to assess how policy translates into program artifacts and decisions. We use Policy Scenario Analysis to examine whether the SWP-centered governance stack provides sufficient actionable support for AI acquisition. The governance stack provides a viable foundation for iterative delivery and AI testing. However, we identify a recurring actionability problem in the core guidance. AI-specific controls for data provenance, lifecycle management, and human oversight remain distributed across supplemental documents rather than embedded in the program-facing mechanisms through which SWP is executed. This disconnect leaves program offices reliant on inconsistent local interpretation. We conclude by recommending an AI-supporting sub-path and targeted artifact refinements to better bridge this policy-to-artifact gap.

### [14] [Socratic-SWE: Self-Evolving Coding Agents via Trace-Derived Agent Skills](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07412v1)
*Chuan Xiao,Zhengbo Jiao,Shaobo Wang,Wei Wang,Bing Zhao,Hu Wei,Linfeng Zhang,Lin Qu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Socratic-SWE框架，利用智能体的历史解决轨迹自我进化，生成有针对性的修复任务，显著提升软件工程智能体的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有合成数据方法生成的SWE任务与智能体弱点无关，限制了训练效果；需一种自适应任务生成方法。

Method: 通过闭环自我进化框架，将历史轨迹提炼为结构化技能，指导生成真实仓库中的修复任务，经执行验证和求解器梯度对齐奖励筛选，用于更新求解器。

Result: 在多个基准测试上，Socratic-SWE在相同计算预算下持续优于基线，在SWE-bench Verified上达到50.40%。

Conclusion: 解决轨迹可作为自我进化SWE智能体的可扩展基础。

中文摘要：基于LLM的软件工程智能体已成为现实世界语言模型能力的核心测试平台，然而它们的训练仍然受到高质量软件工程任务可用性的限制。现有的合成数据方法通常通过固定的突变或缺陷注入程序创建任务，使得生成的分布很大程度上独立于智能体自身的弱点和训练进度。我们提出了Socratic-SWE，一个闭环自我进化框架，它将智能体历史解决轨迹重新用作训练信号的来源。Socratic-SWE并不将轨迹仅视为奖励计算的证据，而是将其提炼为结构化的智能体技能，总结重复出现的失败和有效修复模式。这些技能随后指导在真实仓库中生成有针对性的修复任务。候选任务通过基于执行的验证进行检查，并通过求解器梯度对齐奖励进行评分，从而保留的任务既可验证又有助于改进求解器。更新后的求解器产生新的轨迹，使得任务课程能够在连续轮次中自适应。在SWE-bench Verified、SWE-bench Lite、SWE-bench Pro和Terminal-Bench 2.0上，Socratic-SWE在相同计算预算下持续优于自我进化基线，经过三次迭代后达到SWE-bench Verified上50.40%的准确率。这些结果表明，解决轨迹可以作为自我进化软件工程智能体的可扩展基础。

Original abstract: LLM-driven software engineering agents have become a central testbed for real-world language-model capability, yet their training remains limited by the availability of high-quality SWE tasks. Existing synthetic data methods typically create tasks through fixed mutation or bug-injection procedures, making the resulting distributions largely independent of the agent's own weaknesses and training progress. We introduce Socratic-SWE, a closed-loop self-evolution framework that reuses the agent's historical solving traces as a source of training signal. Rather than treating traces only as evidence for reward computation, Socratic-SWE distills them into structured agent skills that summarize recurring failures and effective repair patterns. These skills then guide the generation of targeted repair tasks in real repositories. Candidate tasks are checked through execution-based validation and scored with a solver-gradient alignment reward, so that the retained tasks are both verifiable and useful for improving the Solver. The updated Solver produces new traces, enabling the task curriculum to adapt over successive rounds. Across SWE-bench Verified, SWE-bench Lite, SWE-bench Pro, and Terminal-Bench 2.0, Socratic-SWE consistently improves over self-evolving baselines under the same compute budget, reaching 50.40% on SWE-bench Verified after three iterations. These results suggest that solving traces can serve as a scalable substrate for self-evolving SWE agents.

</details>

Result: 新样本中编码代理采用率是之前的两倍以上，且AI辅助提交比例更高，表明采用强度显著提高。

Conclusion: 编码代理在GitHub新项目中的采用率和强度显著增加，且实际采用可能超过检测到的水平。

Original abstract: In previous work, we investigated the adoption of coding agents in GitHub projects, finding that it was very significant. We also find that the adoption is significantly more intensive, as the proportion of AI-assisted commits is sensibly higher, despite strong signs that we do not detect all of it.

### [16] [The Windows IOCTL Census: A Corpus-Scale, Multi-Architecture Database of the Driver Control-Code Surface](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07732v1)
*Michael J. Bommarito*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过静态分析恢复27,087个Windows驱动程序的IOCTL攻击面，构建了首个全面的可查询数据库，并用LLM进行排序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究虽有扫描工具和恶意驱动列表，但缺乏对Windows驱动IOCTL攻击面本身的整体地图。

Method: 采用确定性、架构无关的静态分析，读取提升后的中间表示以恢复控制代码分发攻击面；在64位上额外分析处理程序可达性、污点和调用图；利用LLM对可达处理程序进行优先级排序。

Result: 成功恢复80%语料库（27,087个驱动）的攻击面，生成包含310万个控制代码、818万个函数等数据的公开数据集。

Conclusion: 提供了首个Windows驱动IOCTL攻击面的系统级地图，作为公共数据集可推动更深入的安全研究。

中文摘要：Windows驱动程序通过I/O控制（IOCTL）代码暴露其内核，而未经检查的缓冲区长度可能将一个非特权调用转化为内核写入。研究社区对此攻击面有强大的扫描工具和一份已知恶意驱动列表，但缺乏攻击面本身的地图。我们构建了这样一张地图。Windows IOCTL Census是一个可查询的数据库，包含了27,087个已签名Windows驱动的控制代码分发攻击面，通过一次确定性、架构无关的扫描恢复，无需符号执行。通过读取提升后的中间表示而非运行符号引擎，它能够恢复语料库中80%的驱动在x86和x64上的分发攻击面，包括现有扫描工具无法处理的32位部分。在64位路径上，它还增加了处理程序可达性、污点分析和调用图。一个LLM对可达处理程序进行排序以便分类。我们将该普查作为公开数据集发布，包含数千万行数据：27,087个二进制文件、310万个解码控制代码、818万个函数和1595万个调用边。

Original abstract: A Windows driver exposes its kernel through I/O control (IOCTL) codes, and a single unchecked length on the buffer behind one turns an unprivileged call into a kernel write. The research community has strong scanners for this surface and a curated list of known-bad drivers, but no map of the surface itself. We build that map. The Windows IOCTL Census is a queryable database of the control-code dispatch surface of 27,087 signed Windows drivers, recovered by one deterministic, architecture-neutral pass with no symbolic execution. Reading a lifted intermediate representation instead of running a symbolic engine lets it recover a dispatch surface for 80% of the corpus across x86 and x64, including the 32-bit half existing scanners abort on. On the 64-bit lane it adds handler reachability, taint, and the call graph. An LLM ranks the reachable handlers for triage. We release the census as a public dataset of tens of millions of rows: 27,087 binaries, 3.1M decoded control codes, 8.18M functions, and 15.95M call edges.

</details>


### [17] [Sensitivity Analysis White Paper](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07809v1)
*Nate Bade,Lindsay Erickson*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过文献综述，将局部与全局方法、方差基方法、筛选法、导数法及不确定性量化工具等主要方法分类，并关联至因子优先排序、因子固定、方差减少、因子映射等分析目标，同时引入敏感性审计作为补充。

Result: 构建了一个涵盖多种敏感性分析方法及其目标匹配的框架，并强调了敏感性审计在透明度和负责任模型使用中的作用。

Conclusion: 该框架有助于指导复杂仿真（尤其军事领域）中敏感性分析方法的选取与应用，并倡导结合敏感性审计以提升决策支持的可信度。

中文摘要：敏感性分析是仿真决策支持的重要组成部分，因为它帮助分析者在不确定性下确定哪些输入对模型结果的影响最强。本文组织广泛的敏感性分析文献，形成一个用于复杂仿真环境的连贯框架，特别关注军事应用。我们回顾了主要的方法类别，包括局部和全局方法、基于方差的技术、筛选方法、基于导数的方法和不确定性量化工具，并将它们与常见的分析目标（如因子优先排序、因子固定、方差减少和因子映射）联系起来。本文还讨论了敏感性审计作为补充视角，强调透明度、假设跟踪以及在决策相关环境中负责任的模型使用。

Original abstract: Sensitivity analysis is an important component of simulation-based decision support because it helps analysts determine which inputs most strongly influence model outcomes under uncertainty. This paper organizes the broad sensitivity analysis literature into a coherent framework for use in complex simulation settings, with particular attention to military applications. We review major classes of methods, including local and global approaches, variance-based techniques, screening methods, derivative-based methods, and uncertainty quantification tools, and relate them to common analytical objectives such as factor prioritization, factor fixing, variance reduction, and factor mapping. The paper also discusses sensitivity auditing as a complementary perspective that emphasizes transparency, assumption tracking, and responsible use of models in decision-relevant settings.

### [18] [Jas: AI-Paired Engineering as a Revival of N-Version Programming](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07828v1)
*Jason Hickey*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: AI配对软件工程结合YAML规范和差分测试，使单个开发者在120小时内完成五个平台的矢量应用移植，复兴了N-版本编程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索AI配对软件工程是否能使单个开发者完成传统上需要多人年的工作，并验证N-版本编程的现代可行性。

Method: 使用AI辅助实现，同时采用精确的可执行YAML规范作为唯一真实来源，并通过并行实现进行差分测试；单一开发者进行多平台移植。

Result: 五个端口共享23,000行规范，每个端口的本地代码从0到约95,000行不等，整个项目耗时约120个晚上。

Conclusion: 在YAML规范和差分测试的保障下，AI配对工程使单人完成大规模多平台开发成为可能，验证了N-版本编程的复兴价值。

中文摘要：我报告了一个AI配对软件工程的案例研究：一个矢量插图应用程序在Rust、Swift、OCaml、Python和基于浏览器的平台上的五个工作端口，由一个开发者在大约120个晚上完成。该方法将AI辅助实现与两个保障措施相结合——一个精确的可执行YAML规范作为唯一真实来源，以及作为内置差分测试层的并行实现。五个端口共享23,000行的规范；每个端口的本地代码范围从0到大约95,000行，反映了规范的逃生口。我认为，在这两个保障措施条件下，AI配对工程使得通常需要多个开发者年才能完成的工作范围变得可行，并将该方法论视为N-版本编程的复兴，这是一种因成本原因在20世纪80年代被放弃、但AI改变了这一状况的方法。论文报告了具体的成果以及单一开发者案例研究的诚实局限性。

Original abstract: I report a case study in AI-paired software engineering: five working ports of a vector illustration application across Rust, Swift, OCaml, Python, and browser-based platforms, built by a single developer in approximately 120 evening hours. The methodology pairs AI-assisted implementation with two safeguards -- a precise executable YAML specification serving as the single source of truth, and parallel implementations functioning as a built-in differential-testing layer. The five ports share a 23{,}000-line specification; per-port native code ranges from 0 to roughly 95{,}000 lines, reflecting the specification's escape hatch. I argue that AI-paired engineering, conditional on these two safeguards, makes feasible scope of work that conventionally requires multiple developer-years, and frame the methodology as a revival of N-version programming, a 1980s approach abandoned on cost grounds that AI changes. The paper reports concrete artifacts and honest limitations of the single-developer case study.

</details>


### [19] [Academic Integrity and Emotional Responses to Inappropriate LLM Use in Software Engineering Education](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07830v1)
*Ronnie de Souza Santos,Italo Santos,Giuseppe Destefanis,Cleyton Magalhaes,Mairieli Wessel*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 学生使用LLM后情感反应各异，冷漠最常见，内疚焦虑与道德不适相关，解脱满足多出现在截止日期压力或指导不清时。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究软件工程学生在使用LLM进行学术不当行为后的情感体验，以理解学术诚信在技术环境下的复杂性。

Method: 对116名本科生进行横截面调查，收集他们使用LLM后自认为学术不当的情感描述。

Result: 情感反应异质，冷漠最频繁，内疚焦虑与道德及处罚担忧相关，解脱满足与截止日期和模糊指导相关。

Conclusion: 学生在使用LLM后的情感体验多样，需要更多关注学术诚信教育中的情感维度。

中文摘要：高等教育中的学术诚信日益受到复杂的社会技术环境影响，这些环境以自动化工具、不断变化的制度实践和加剧的绩效压力为特征。在此背景下，大型语言模型（LLM）在软件工程教育中变得越来越普遍，进一步模糊了可接受帮助和作者身份的界限。本研究调查了软件工程学生如何描述他们在以自认为学术不当的方式使用LLM后的情感体验。我们对116名本科生进行了横截面调查。结果显示情感反应具有异质性。冷漠最为常见，包括那些认识到学习和学术地位风险的学生。内疚和焦虑与道德不适及对处罚的担忧有关。解脱和满足感主要出现在截止日期驱动和指导不明确的情境中。

Original abstract: Academic integrity in higher education is increasingly shaped by complex socio-technical environments marked by automated tools, evolving institutional practices, and heightened performance pressures. Within this context, large language models (LLMs) are becoming prevalent in software engineering education, further blurring boundaries around acceptable assistance and authorship. This study investigates how software engineering students describe their emotional experiences after using LLMs in ways they perceive as academically inappropriate. We conducted a cross-sectional survey with 116 undergraduate students. Results show emotionally heterogeneous responses. Indifference was most frequent, including among students who recognized risks to learning and academic standing. Guilt and anxiety were reported in relation to moral discomfort and concern about penalties. Relief and satisfaction were evident primarily in deadline-driven contexts and situations of unclear guidance.

</details>

Original abstract: This paper presents SLRMentor, a conversational assistant designed to support both learning about the systematic literature review process and the execution of planning activities in software engineering. The tool offers general guidance on SLR methodology and supports key planning tasks, including search string construction and reasoning about inclusion and exclusion criteria, with explanations grounded in established SLR guidelines. A pilot validation with graduate students suggests that SLRMentor helps clarify the SLR process and planning decisions, lowers initial barriers for novice researchers, and supports learning while still requiring active methodological judgment.

### [21] [Cherry-pick Override: Unsafe Directional Commitment in LLM Judges under Mixed Evidence](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07834v1)
*Haoran Xu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了LLM裁判在混合证据下做出方向性承诺的Cherry-pick Override问题，并论证需要一个外部承诺控制层将裁决生成与授权分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM裁判在混合证据下不安全地做出方向性承诺，现有单通道修复无法彻底解决，需要新的控制机制。

Method: 定义CCO失败，设计同分母诊断协议、匹配覆盖率的自助法及随机否决零假设，并评估多种修复方法的残余失败，最后提出双通道参考探针和外部承诺控制层。

Result: 三选项裁判在AVerTiC上84%以上返回方向性裁决；多数投票放大方向性但非完全有效；各单通道修复均有残余失败；双通道探针达到更好性能且选择性显著。

Conclusion: 应引入外部承诺控制层，分离生成与授权，使用结构证据和置信度作为正交通道，NO-COMMIT作为路由控制器状态。

中文摘要：LLM裁判越来越多地将裁决转化为系统承诺。在混合证据（既有支持又有反驳来源的声明）下这是不安全的：当模式暴露CONFLICTING作为授权的非方向性裁决时，返回SUPPORTS/REFUTES是一种未经授权的方向性承诺，我们将这种失败命名为Cherry-pick Override（CCO）。我们在明确的任务合同下定义CCO，并使用同分母诊断协议、匹配覆盖率的自助法以及苹果对苹果的随机否决零假设来报告它。在AVerTiC的Conflicting子集（N_C=150）上，三选项裁判对超过84%的混合证据声明返回方向性裁决；在类型化模式下，三裁判多数投票在AVerTiC上放大了冲突时的方向性（0.887 vs. 0.840；95% CI [+0.013, +0.080]），但在VitaminC-Mixed上未复现。在常见单通道修复（类型化词汇、面板聚合、置信度阈值、仅验证器过滤）的干预阶梯上行走，每种方法都留下了不同的残余失败：面板聚合在48%的CCO案例中抑制了单个裁判的CONFLICTING异议；面板在方向性上校准良好（纯S/R的ECE=0.07），因此置信度无法在操作上区分CCO与正确的方向性承诺；验证器作为分类器将纯证据准确率几乎减半。一个最小双通道参考探针达到单通道无法达到的工作点；在随机否决零假设下，其对CONFLICTING的提升在AVerTiC上是结构性的（经验p<1/2001），在VitaminC-Mixed上方向相同但较弱，这是一个选择性结果而非幅度结果。我们主张一个外部承诺控制层，将裁决生成与承诺授权分离，使用结构证据和置信度作为正交通道，NO-COMMIT作为路由控制器状态。

Original abstract: LLM judges increasingly turn verdicts into system commitments. Under mixed evidence (claims with both supporting and refuting sources) this is unsafe: when the schema exposes CONFLICTING as the authorized non-directional verdict, returning SUPPORTS/REFUTES is an unauthorized directional commitment, a failure we name Cherry-pick Override (CCO). We define CCO under an explicit task contract and report it with a same-denominator diagnostic protocol paired with matched-coverage bootstrap and an apples-to-apples random-veto null. On AVeriTeC's Conflicting subset (N_C = 150), three-option judges return a directional verdict on more than 84% of mixed-evidence claims; under the typed schema, three-judge majority voting amplifies direction-on-conflict on AVeriTeC (0.887 vs. 0.840; 95% CI [+0.013, +0.080]) but does not replicate on VitaminC-Mixed. Walking an intervention ladder of common single-channel fixes (typed vocabulary, panel aggregation, confidence thresholding, validator-only filtering), each leaves a distinct residual failure: panel aggregation suppresses single-judge CONFLICTING dissent in 48% of CCO cases; the panel is well-calibrated for direction (ECE = 0.07 on pure-S/R) so confidence cannot operationally separate CCO from correct directional commits; validator-as-classifier nearly halves pure-evidence accuracy. A minimal two-channel reference probe reaches operating points neither single channel reaches; under the random-veto null its promotion to CONFLICTING is structurally targeted on AVeriTeC (empirical p < 1/2001) and weaker but in the same direction on VitaminC-Mixed, a selectivity result rather than a magnitude one. We argue for an external commitment-control layer that separates verdict generation from commitment authorization, using structural evidence and confidence as orthogonal channels and NO-COMMIT as a routed controller state.

</details>


### [22] [A Preliminary Model for Managing Technical Debt in an Agile Environment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07859v1)
*Pedro E. Colla*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出一个敏捷环境中管理非自愿技术债务的模型，通过动态策略平衡新开发与修复，并验证了其经济直觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在敏捷环境中，技术债务管理缺乏综合考虑积压、债务、速度和经济价值的模型，现有策略未考虑跨期价值决策。

Method: 构建动态模型，区分功能债务与缺陷，定义生产力下降为利息，提出动态策略uk，引入递减边际价值，扩展至离散非齐次项，通过敏感性分析和蒙特卡洛模拟验证。

Result: 模型行为与经济学直觉一致，显示了动态策略的合理性。

Conclusion: 该模型是初步的，存在宏观性、对稳定参数的依赖、跨期理性假设和弱耦合要求等局限。

中文摘要：本文提出了一种在敏捷环境中管理非自愿技术债务的初步模型，通过综合方式构建了积压工作、债务、速度和经济价值之间的动态关系。该工作将已启动但未完成的功能债务与单纯的缺陷积压和返工区分开来，将生产力下降解释为技术债务的利息，并推导出天真的最大修复策略以展示其相对于跨期价值决策的局限性。在此基础上，提出了一种动态策略uk来平衡新开发和修复；引入了递减边际价值结构；并将模型扩展到离散的、非齐次的项目。通过敏感性分析和蒙特卡洛模拟进行的探索性验证显示了与模型经济直觉一致的行为。最后，明确了该公式的局限性：其宏观性质、对组织稳定参数的依赖、对跨期理性的假设以及对故事之间弱耦合的要求。

Original abstract: This paper presents a preliminary model for managing involuntary technical debt in agile environments by formulating, in an integrated way, the dynamics among backlog, debt, velocity, and economic value. The work distinguishes initiated but unfinished functional debt from a simple defect back log and from rework, interprets productivity degradation as technical-debt interest, and derives the naive maximum-remediation policy in order to show its limitations against an intertemporal value-based decision. On this basis, a dynamic policy uk is proposed to balance new development and remediation; a decreasing marginal-value structure is incorporated; and the model is extended to discrete, inhomogeneous items. Exploratory validation through sensitivity analysis and MonteCarlo simulation shows behavior consistent with the economic intuition of the model. Finally, the limits of the formulation are made explicit: its macroscopic nature, its dependence on organizationally stable parameters, its assumption of intertemporal rationality, and its requirement of weak coupling among stories.

### [23] [DD-GEPA: Prompt Optimization for Dialogue Disentanglement Focusing on Task Instruction and Utterance Representation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07894v1)
*Naoki Takada,Tatsunori Mori*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了一种自动提示优化方法，通过分解提示为三个组件并使用GEPA优化，提升了LLM在对话解缠任务上的准确率，可超越手工提示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在对话解缠任务上准确率较低，而手动设计提示效果有限，因此需要自动优化提示以提升性能。

Method: 将提示分解为任务指令、话语表示和输出指令三个组件，并使用GEPA优化方法进行自动优化。

Result: 在基准数据集上，优化后的提示相比原始提示提高了对话解缠准确率，并超越了手工制作的提示。

Conclusion: 自动提示优化能够有效提升LLM在对话解缠任务上的表现，且优化后的提示优于手工提示。

中文摘要：多方聊天通常包含交错对话，因为多个参与者可以同时讨论不同的话题。对话解缠通过将纠缠的语句序列分离成连贯的对话来解决这个问题。虽然大型语言模型（LLM）对此任务有前景，但它们仍然难以处理对话解缠，且准确率较低。本文提出了一种基于LLM的对话解缠的自动提示优化方法。我们将提示分解为三个组成部分：任务指令、话语表示和输出指令，并使用GEPA（一种用于复合AI系统的优化方法）对它们进行优化。在基准数据集上的实验表明，优化后的提示相比原始提示提高了对话解缠的准确率，并且可以超越手工制作的提示。

Original abstract: Multi-party chat often contains interleaved dialogues because multiple participants can discuss different topics at the same time. Dialogue disentanglement addresses this problem by separating an entangled utterance sequence into coherent dialogues. While large language models (LLMs) are promising for this task, they still struggle with dialogue disentanglement and achieve low accuracy. This paper proposes an automatic prompt optimization for LLM based dialogue disentanglement. We decompose the prompt into three components: task instruction, utterance representation, and output instruction, and optimize them using GEPA, an optimization method for compound AI systems. Experiments on benchmark datasets show that the optimized prompts improve dialogue disentanglement accuracy over the original prompts and can surpass hand crafted prompts.

### [24] [AdMem: Advanced Memory for Task-solving Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06787v1)
*Runzhe Wang,Huilin Lu,Shengjie Liu,Li Dong,Jason Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出统一自动记忆框架，包含语义、情景、程序记忆和多agent架构，可迁移到coding agent的记忆管理。

TL;DR: 提出一个统一的自动记忆框架，整合语义、情节和程序记忆，通过双层存储和多智能体架构实现自适应检索与长期记忆管理，在长多轮任务中提升鲁棒性和成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM工具使用在长期任务中受限于记忆能力不足，尤其是缺乏对失败案例的处理和在线可扩展性。

Method: 设计一个统一自动记忆框架，包含短期和长期存储，集成语义、情节和程序记忆；采用多智能体架构（actor、memory、critic agents）实现自动记忆生成、奖励标注和自适应检索；长期记忆通过基于奖励的评估、合并和剪枝管理。

Result: 在多种环境中，该方法在长多轮任务上的鲁棒性和成功率优于现有基线。

Conclusion: 全面、自适应的记忆对于提升LLM智能体的能力至关重要，该框架展示了在复杂任务中持续改进的潜力。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）作为使用工具的智能体显示出前景，但在需要记忆、组织和重用知识的长期任务中仍然受限。先前的记忆方法旨在解决这一问题，但主要侧重于存储事实信息。最近关于程序性记忆的工作改进了任务重用，但往往简化为重放过去的成功，而未处理失败案例或在线可扩展性。我们引入了一个统一且自动的记忆框架，该框架整合了语义、情节和程序性记忆，采用结合短期和长期存储的双层设计。一个由行动者、记忆和评论家智能体组成的多智能体架构实现了自动记忆生成、奖励注释和自适应检索。长期记忆通过基于奖励的评估、合并和修剪进行管理，确保可扩展性和持续改进。跨多种环境的实验表明，与现有基线相比，我们的方法在长多轮任务上提高了鲁棒性和成功率。这项工作强调了全面、自适应记忆对于推进基于LLM的智能体的重要性。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) show promise as tool-using agents but remain limited in long-horizon tasks that require remembering, organizing, and reusing knowledge. Prior memory approaches aim to resolve the situation, but mainly focus on storing factual information. Recent work on procedural memory improves task reuse, yet often reduces to replaying past successes without addressing failure cases or online scalability. We introduce a unified and automatic memory framework that integrates semantic, episodic, and procedural memory in a bi-level design combining short-term and long-term stores. A multi-agent architecture with actor, memory, and critic agents enables automatic memory generation, reward annotation, and adaptive retrieval. Long-term memory is managed through reward-based evaluation, merging, and pruning, ensuring scalability and continual improvement. Experiments across various environments show that our approach improves robustness and success on long multi-turn tasks compared to existing baselines. This work highlights the importance of comprehensive, adaptive memory for advancing LLM-based agents.

### [25] [Workflow-to-Skill: Skill Creation via Routing-Workflow-Semantics-Attachments Decomposition](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06893v1)
*Yuyang Zhang,Xinyuan Han,Xudong Jiang,Run Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出从轨迹到技能的自动构造框架，涉及工作流分解与验证，对coding agent的技能学习有直接迁移价值。

TL;DR: 提出W2S框架，通过RWSA中间表示从异构交互证据自动构建技能，在70个技能上提升行为重放一致性10.5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手动编写高质量技能成本高，且从痕迹到技能的构建不是简单摘要，因为痕迹碎片化、冗余、遗漏安全关键行为。

Method: 引入RWSA中间表示（工作流结构、执行语义、运行时附件），基于此提出W2S框架（分段、归纳、对齐、协调、压缩）。

Result: 在70个技能上，W2S比基于摘要/提示的基线提高行为重放一致性10.5%。

Conclusion: 痕迹应视为可执行的运行时规范，而非可压缩文本。

中文摘要：大型语言模型代理越来越依赖技能（Skills）来编码程序性知识，然而高质量的技能手工编写成本高昂。本文研究从异构交互证据（包括演示、代理轨迹、工具痕迹和执行日志）中自动构建技能。我们认为，从痕迹到技能的构建并非简单的摘要任务，因为痕迹是碎片化、冗余的，并且可能遗漏罕见但安全关键的行为。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了RWSA，一种面向工作流的中间表示，它将技能分解为工作流结构、执行语义和运行时附件，捕获任务分解、控制流、验证、安全性、回滚和状态管理。基于RWSA，我们提出了W2S框架，该框架对痕迹进行分段、归纳局部技能草稿、对齐共享结构、协调分支，并在保留证据和置信度注释的同时压缩冗余。在70个技能上的实验表明，W2S将行为重放一致性比基于摘要和提示的基线提高了10.5%，强调了需要将痕迹视为可执行的运行时规范，而不是可压缩的文本。

Original abstract: Large language model agents increasingly rely on Skills to encode procedural knowledge, yet high-quality Skills remain costly to hand-write. This paper studies automatic Skill construction from heterogeneous interaction evidence, including demonstrations, agent trajectories, tool traces, and execution logs. We argue that trace-to-skill construction is not simple summarization tasks, because traces are fragmented, redundant, and may miss rare but safety-critical behaviors. To address this, we introduce RWSA, a workflow-oriented intermediate representation that decomposes Skills into Workflow structure, execution Semantics, and runtime Attachments, capturing task decomposition, control flow, verification, safety, rollback, and state management. Building on RWSA, we propose W2S, a framework that segments traces, induces local Skill drafts, aligns shared structures, reconciles branches, and compresses redundancy while preserving evidence and confidence annotations. Experiments on 70 Skills show that W2S improves behavioral replay consistency by 10.5% over summarization- and prompting-based baselines, highlighting the need to treat traces as executable runtime specifications rather than compressible text.

</details>


### [26] [Declarative Skills for AI Agents in Knowledge-Grounded Tool-Use Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06923v1)
*M. Danish Lim,I. Danial Bin Sharudin,Wen Han Chen,Cedric Lim,Laura Wynter*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文比较了声明式、命令式和基线AI智能体在客户服务场景中的编排效果，发现检索质量是关键瓶颈，高检索质量下声明式技能有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在非结构化知识库上使用工具的AI智能体的有效编排机制，特别是比较声明式与命令式方法的优劣。

Method: 将三种智能体形式化为分散部分可观察马尔可夫决策过程中的策略类，并在五个语言模型和两种检索设置下进行实证比较。

Result: 检索质量是主要瓶颈：低检索时所有智能体性能下降；高检索时声明式智能体提升程序任务准确性并减少编排错误。

Conclusion: 声明式技能在高检索质量下有效，命令式状态机不可靠，检索质量是核心因素。

中文摘要：我们研究在非结构化知识库上的真实客户服务工作流中，使用工具的AI智能体的编排机制。我们认为声明式智能体——即在系统提示中附加自然语言技能文件的AI智能体——是一种有效的编排范式。具体地，我们比较了(i) 一个声明式智能体，它在推理时读取三个特定领域的技能文件并自行决定其控制流；(ii) 一个基于具有显式阶段的程序化状态机的基础式智能体；以及(iii) 一个基于τ-Knowledge基准智能体的无脚手架基线智能体。我们的基础式智能体受递归语言模型和基于图的编排框架中的外部化控制推理启发。我们将这三个智能体形式化为分散部分可观察马尔可夫决策过程中的策略类，并分析它们的信息论和结构特性；然后我们在五个语言模型和两种检索机制上实证测试了预测的差异。我们的结果表明，检索质量是AI智能体的主要瓶颈：当证据不完整或偏斜时，所有智能体都会大幅退化，技能文件无法恢复损失的性能。然而，在高检索质量下，声明式技能持续提高了程序任务的准确性并减少了编排错误，而基础式状态机的脆弱性并不能可靠地提高任务成功率或合规性。

Original abstract: We study orchestration mechanisms for tool-using AI agents in realistic customer-service workflows over an unstructured knowledge base. We argue that declarative agents -- AI agents equipped with natural-language skill files appended to the system prompt -- are an effective orchestration paradigm. Concretely, we compare (i) a DeclarativeAgent that reads three domain-specific skill files at inference time and decides its own control flow, (ii) an ImperativeAgent based on a programmatic state machine with explicit phases, and (iii) an unscaffolded baseline agent modeled after the $τ$-Knowledge benchmark agent. Our ImperativeAgent is motivated by externalised-control inference as in Recursive Language Models and graph-based orchestration frameworks. We formalise the three agents as policy classes within a decentralised partially-observable Markov decision process and analyse their information-theoretic and structural properties; we then test the predicted differences empirically on five language models and two retrieval regimes. Our results show that retrieval quality is a dominant bottleneck for AI agents: when evidence is incomplete or skewed, all agents degrade substantially, and skill files cannot recover lost performance. Under high-quality retrieval, however, declarative skills consistently improve accuracy on procedural tasks and reduce orchestration errors, while the imperative state machine's brittleness does not reliably improve task success or compliance.

### [27] [Quantum-Inspired Trace-Augmented Evidence Selection for Reasoning over Structured Hypothesis Spaces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06941v1)
*Laura Wynter,Nirvik Sahoo,Paul Griffin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 将CoT推理片段选择建模为组合优化，可启发agent的证据聚合与反思机制。

TL;DR: EP-HUBO通过组合优化聚合思维链片段，在证据密集型法律任务中优于多数投票，保留少数正确假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多数投票忽略证据强度，导致少数正确假设被淹没；法律领域对证据质量敏感，需要更好的聚合方法。

Method: 将CoT片段选择建模为组合优化问题，使用高阶二元优化（HUBO）基于证据质量权重（相关性、特异性、独特性）求解，并委托前沿模型做最终裁决。

Result: 在两个证据密集型法律基准上，EP-HUBO在模拟退火和量子计算上均表现出有效聚合，保留少数正确假设。

Conclusion: HUBO风格的优化为推理片段聚合提供了原则性方法，在低污染领域最有价值。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）现在能够以人类水平或更高水平解决一系列专家级考试，但在法律等专业化、证据密集的领域仍然脆弱。在这些任务中，错误不仅源于世界知识的空白，还源于证据之间的细微差别以及证据使用的不一致性。最常用的对采样思维链（CoT）轨迹的聚合方法——多数投票——返回最流行的答案，而不考虑其证据是否实际上最强。我们提出将CoT推理片段的选择视为一个显式的组合优化问题，使有充分证据支持的少数假设能够压倒嘈杂的多数，并在对证据质量特别敏感的法律推理基准上评估该方法。我们引入EP-HUBO（证据池高阶二元优化），它使用小型本地模型生成多个CoT轨迹，将片段解析为每个假设的证据池，使用质量衍生权重（相关性、特异性、独特性）求解每个池的高阶无约束二元优化，并将每个问题的单一裁决调用委托给前沿模型。我们在两个证据密集型法律基准上评估了EP-HUBO，同时使用经典硬件上的模拟退火和Quantum Computing Inc.的Dirac-3光子熵量子机。HUBO风格的优化提供了一种原则性的方式来聚合推理片段，同时保留少数但正确的假设，并且在污染较低、前沿模型尚未吸收基准材料的领域中最为有价值。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) now solve a wide range of expert-level exams at or above human level, yet remain brittle on specialised, evidence-intensive domains such as law. On these tasks, errors arise not only from gaps in world knowledge but also from subtle distinctions between pieces of evidence and inconsistent use of supporting evidence. The most common aggregator over sampled chain-of-thought (CoT) traces, majority vote, returns the most popular answer regardless of whether its evidence is actually strongest. We propose to treat the selection of CoT reasoning fragments into a set of evidence as an explicit combinatorial optimisation problem, allowing well-supported but minority hypotheses to override noisy majorities, and to evaluate the approach on legal-reasoning benchmarks that are particularly sensitive to evidence quality. We introduce EP-HUBO (Evidence Pool Higher-Order Binary Optimisation), which generates multiple CoT traces with a small local model, parses fragments into per-hypothesis evidence pools, solves a higher-order unconstrained binary optimisation per pool with quality-derived weights (relevance, specificity, distinctiveness), and delegates a single adjudication call per question to a frontier model. We evaluate EP-HUBO on two evidence-intensive legal benchmarks using both simulated annealing on classical hardware and the Dirac-3 photonic entropy-quantum machine from Quantum Computing Inc. HUBO-style optimisation gives a principled way to aggregate reasoning fragments while preserving minority-but-correct hypotheses, and is most valuable in low-contamination domains where frontier models have not already absorbed the benchmark material.

### [28] [NAVI-Orbital: First In-Orbit Demonstration of a Zero-Shot Vision-Language Model for Autonomous Earth Observation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18271v1)
*Juan Manuel Delfa Victoria,Taran Cyriac John,Andrew W. Herson*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 在轨VLM系统使用LangGraph多agent协调，直接展示agent部署与推理规划。

TL;DR: 首次在轨演示了视觉-语言模型，通过语义压缩实现星载自主多模态推理，减少下行带宽需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地球观测数据生成速度超过下行带宽和人工处理能力，导致星载采集与地面情报之间的差距扩大。

Method: 部署NAVI-Orbital系统，使用Gemma 3视觉-语言模型进行星载多模态推理，通过自然语言提示重新任务，并由LangGraph状态机协调检测和对话代理。

Result: 地面基准准确率88.16%，平板卫星验证成功，在轨捕获新图像实现硬件加速GPU推理且无需微调。

中文摘要：随着地球观测数据的生成速度超过下行链路带宽和人工处理能力，星载采集与可操作地面情报之间的差距日益扩大。本文介绍了NAVI-Orbital，一个部署在低地球轨道（LEO）航天器上的软件系统。2026年4月16日，NAVI-Orbital实现了据作者所知首次在轨演示的视觉-语言模型，完全在星上进行自主多模态推理。NAVI-Orbital使用本地视觉-语言模型（Gemma 3）对每个捕获场景进行分类，生成其内容及其特征之间关系的文本描述，并通过自然语言对话响应操作员的后续问题。该系统通过纯英语提示重新调整任务，取代传统的命令序列，并由基于图的状态机（LangGraph）协调专门的检测和对话代理。地面基准测试（在7960张图像的精选AID基准上准确率达到88.16%）、平板卫星验证以及实时在轨捕获的新获取、以前未见过的地球图像（包括未经校正的YAM-9图像，在星上通过硬件加速GPU推理进行处理，且未对飞行仪器进行微调）的结果证明了在卫星级边缘计算机上运行基础模型的可行性，通过在轨语义压缩颠覆了传统的采集然后全部下行的带宽模式。

Original abstract: As Earth Observation data generation outpaces downlink bandwidth and human-in-the-loop processing, a widening gap has emerged between onboard collection and actionable ground intelligence. This paper presents NAVI-Orbital, a software system deployed on a Low Earth Orbit (LEO) spacecraft. On April 16, 2026, NAVI-Orbital achieved what is, to the authors' knowledge, the first in-orbit demonstration of a vision-language model performing autonomous multi-modal inference entirely onboard. NAVI-Orbital uses a local vision-language model (Gemma 3) to classify each captured scene, produce a text description of its content and the relationships between its features, and respond to operator follow-up via natural-language dialogue. The system is re-tasked through plain-English prompts in place of conventional command sequences, and is orchestrated by a graph-based state machine (LangGraph) coordinating dedicated agents for detection and dialogue. Results across ground benchmarking (88.16% accuracy on the 7,960-image curated AID benchmark), Flatsat validation, and live in-orbit captures of newly acquired, previously unseen Earth imagery (including uncorrected YAM-9 imagery, processed onboard with hardware-accelerated GPU inference and no fine-tuning for the flight instrument) demonstrate the feasibility of running foundation models on satellite-class edge computers to invert the conventional acquire-then-downlink-everything bandwidth profile through semantic compression of Earth observations in-orbit.

### [29] [Exploring Agentic Tool-Calling Decisions via Uncertainty-Aligned Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06976v1)
*Yijin Zhou,Linqian Zeng,Xiaoya Lu,Wenyuan Xie,Dongrui Liu,Junchi Yan,Jing Shao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出不确定性对齐的强化学习优化agent工具调用决策，方法可迁移。

TL;DR: 提出TRUST方法，通过不确定性量化增强奖励以保持决策不确定性分离，并利用关键轮次注释进行后训练，显著提升LLM智能体工具使用的决策质量和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体在工具使用中常做出次优决策，如错误调用或幻觉响应，且现有方法忽视了决策的不确定性特征，导致过度自信和探索不足。

Method: 提出TRUST，将不确定性量化作为排斥力引入奖励设计以维持不确定性分离，并添加轻量级关键轮次注释进行多轮轨迹的统一后训练。

Result: 在多个工具使用基准上，TRUST一致提升了决策质量和智能体性能，同时保持了更可靠的不确定性估计。

Conclusion: 不确定性量化与奖励设计结合能有效改善智能体工具使用决策，TRUST通过维持不确定性分离和关键轮次注释实现更好性能。

中文摘要：基于大语言模型的智能体经常做出次优的工具使用决策，包括不支持的调用和幻觉性的直接响应，这可能在多步交互中积累错误。现有方法主要通过推理时纠正或基于决策结果和结构化清单的粗粒度奖励信号来改善这些行为，而忽略了智能体决策的不确定性特征。我们观察到，以决策为导向的强化学习往往会削弱正确和错误动作之间的不确定性分离，导致过度自信的错误和较弱的探索信号。因此，我们提出了TRUST，它将不确定性量化引入奖励设计，作为维持不确定性分离的排斥力，并标记了轻量级的关键轮次注释，用于多轮轨迹的统一后训练。在多种工具使用基准上的实验结果表明，TRUST在优化过程中持续提升了决策质量和智能体性能，同时保持了更可靠的不确定性估计。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based agents often make suboptimal tool-use decisions, including unsupported tool invocation and hallucinated direct responses, which may accumulate errors throughout multi-step interactions. Existing approaches mainly improve these behaviors through inference-time correction or coarse-grained reward signals based on decision outcomes and structured checklists, leaving the uncertainty characteristics of agent decisions underexplored. We observe that decision-oriented reinforcement learning tends to weaken the uncertainty separation between correct and incorrect actions, resulting in overconfident mistakes and weaker exploration signals. Therefore, we propose TRUST, which incorporates uncertainty quantification into reward design as a repulsive force for maintaining uncertainty separation, and labels lightweight key-turn annotations for unified post-training of multi-turn trajectories. Experimental results across diverse tool-use benchmarks show that TRUST consistently enhances both decision quality and agent performance while maintaining more reliable uncertainty estimates during optimization.

### [30] [The Sim-to-Real Gap of Foundation Model Agents: A Unified MDP Perspective](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07017v1)
*Xiaoou Liu,Tiejin Chen,Weibo Li,Xiyang Hu,Hua Wei*

TL;DR: 论文提出将基础模型智能体的评估与训练差距形式化为sim-to-real问题，并倡导采用域随机化等成熟解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基础模型智能体在现实部署中面临sim-to-real差距，但社区将其视为新现象，缺乏统一框架和标准化解决方案。

Method: 将差距形式化为围绕马尔可夫决策过程四个要素（观测、动作、转移、奖励）的经典sim-to-real问题，并倡导采用域随机化等成熟解决方案。

Result: 通过多语言工具调用等具体例子，展示了观测空间差距导致语义正确但操作无效的动作。

Conclusion: 该议程推动范式转变，建立统一词汇和标准化压力测试基准，以培育高度可信的智能体，实现可靠现实应用。

中文摘要：基础模型智能体越来越多地被部署用于现实世界的决策制定，但面临着从模拟到现实（sim-to-real）的差距。虽然机器人技术和经典控制拥有成熟的框架来解决这一差距，但基础模型社区却将智能体的鲁棒性视为一个全新的现象。我们的论文提出将基础模型智能体的评估和训练差距形式化为一个经典的sim-to-real问题，完全围绕马尔可夫决策过程的四个要素构建，包括观测、动作、转移和奖励。在本文中，我们设定了一个全面的研究议程，将经典的差异转化为基础模型领域，并倡导采用成熟的解决方案，如域随机化。我们提供了具体的例子，例如一个多语言工具调用，展示了严重的观测空间差距如何导致尽管语义意图正确但操作无效的动作。最终，该议程旨在推动范式转变，产生统一的词汇和标准化的压力测试基准，以培育新一代高度可信的智能体，用于可靠的现实世界应用。

Original abstract: Foundation model agents are increasingly deployed for real-world decision-making, but suffer from the sim-to-real gap. While robotics and classical control have mature frameworks to address this gap, the foundation model community is treating agent robustness as an entirely novel phenomenon. Our paper proposes formalizing the foundation model agent evaluation and training gap as a classical sim-to-real problem structured entirely around the four elements of a Markov Decision Process, including Observation, Action, Transition, and Reward. In this paper, we set a comprehensive research agenda that translates classical discrepancies into the foundation model domain and advocates for adopting established solutions like domain randomization. We provide concrete examples, such as a multilingual tool calling to demonstrate how severe observation space gaps lead to operationally invalid actions despite correct semantic intent. Ultimately, this agenda aims to drive a paradigm shift, yielding a unified vocabulary and standardized stress test benchmarks to foster a new generation of highly trustworthy agents for reliable real-world applications.

### [31] [StainFlow: Entity-Stain Tracking and Evidence Linking for Process Rewards in GUI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07027v2)
*Haojie Hao,Longkun Hao,Yihang Lou,Yan Bai,Zhenyang Li,Zhichao Yang,Dongshuo Huang,Hongyu Lin,Lanqing Hong,Jiakai Wang,Xianglong Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出GUI agent的过程奖励模型，实体追踪与证据链接，直接相关agent方法。

TL;DR: 提出StainFlow模型，通过全局实体污点追踪和局部污点证据链接改进GUI代理的过程奖励，提升在线RL成功率和轨迹判断准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PRM方法在全局里程碑分解上主观且单一，难以适应多种有效路径，且局部判断窗口固定，易遗漏远程关键证据或引入噪声，导致信用分配不准确。

Method: 提出StainFlow，包含全局实体污点追踪模块（客观分离任务阶段）和局部污点证据链接模块（动态构建高密度证据窗口验证关键节点）。

Result: 在AndroidWorld和OGRBench上，在线RL成功率相对提升3.2%，轨迹完成判断准确率相对提升1.8%。

Conclusion: StainFlow通过实体污点流机制有效克服了现有PRM的局限性，显著提升了GUI代理的训练效果。

中文摘要：强化学习（RL）已成为在长时域、随机数字环境中改进GUI代理的一种有前景的方法，但轨迹级成功反馈过于稀疏，无法为中间探索步骤提供可靠的信用分配。为了缓解这一问题，最近的研究引入了过程奖励模型（PRM），通过全局里程碑验证或局部步骤级评估提供更细粒度的训练反馈。然而，这些方法仍然存在两个层级特有的局限性：全局里程碑分解是主观且单一的，难以适应真实GUI任务中多种有效的执行路径，而固定的局部判断窗口可能会遗漏远程关键证据或用无关帧稀释决策信号。受网络流量分析中污点追踪机制的启发，我们提出了StainFlow，一种用于GUI代理的实体污点流过程奖励模型。为了减少全局划分的主观性，我们引入了全局实体污点追踪模块，该模块提取可视觉验证的任务实体，并追踪其污点浓度和状态沿轨迹的演变，从而通过实体证据流的变化客观地分离任务阶段。为了提高局部验证的准确性，我们引入了局部污点证据链接模块。该模块以每个候选关键节点的触发实体为中心，根据其污点浓度和状态变化检索相关步骤，并动态构建高密度证据窗口以验证真正的关键节点。在AndroidWorld和OGRBench上的大量实验表明，StainFlow将在线RL的成功率相对提高了3.2%，轨迹完成判断准确率相对提高了1.8%。

Original abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) has become a promising approach for improving GUI Agents in long-horizon, stochastic digital environments, but trajectory-level success feedback is too sparse to provide reliable credit assignment for intermediate exploration steps. To mitigate this issue, recent studies introduce Process Reward Models (PRMs), which provide finer-grained training feedback through global milestone verification or local step-level evaluation. However, these methods still suffer from two level-specific limitations: global milestone decomposition is subjective and singular, making it difficult to accommodate the multiple valid execution paths in real GUI tasks, while fixed local judging windows may miss long-range key evidence or dilute the decision signal with irrelevant frames. Inspired by stain-tracing mechanisms in network flow analysis, we propose StainFlow, an entity-stain-flow process reward model for GUI Agents. To reduce the subjectivity of global partitioning, we introduce the Global Entity Stain Tracking module, which extracts visually verifiable task entities and tracks how their stain concentrations and states evolve along the trajectory, allowing task phases to be objectively separated by changes in the entity evidence flow. To improve the accuracy of local verification, we introduce the Local Stain Evidence Linking module. Centered on the triggering entities of each candidate key node, it retrieves relevant steps based on their stain concentrations and state changes, and dynamically constructs high-density evidence windows for verifying true key nodes. Extensive experiments on AndroidWorld and OGRBench show that StainFlow relatively improves online RL success by 3.2% and trajectory completion judgment accuracy by 1.8%.

</details>


### [32] [DyCon: Dynamic Reasoning Control via Evolving Difficulty Modeling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07108v2)
*Tengyao Tu,Yulin Li,Hui-Ling Zhen,Libo Qin,Zhoujun Wei,Jinghua Piao,Zhuotao Tian,Yong Li,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM动态推理控制，可减少agent冗余思考

TL;DR: DyCon利用步骤级嵌入动态建模任务难度，无需训练即可控制推理深度，有效减少过度思考，提升效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖静态难度估计或任务特定训练，无法适应推理过程中动态变化的复杂性，导致过度思考问题。

Method: DyCon通过利用LRM的步骤级嵌入显式建模动态任务难度，从而动态控制推理深度。

Result: 在四个模型和十二个基准上，DyCon显著减少了冗余步骤，提升了推理效率，且未牺牲准确性或泛化能力。

Conclusion: DyCon是一种有效的无需训练框架，能动态缓解过度思考问题，提升LLM的推理效率。

中文摘要：大型推理模型（LRMs）的最新进展通过迭代反思、探索和执行复杂任务展示了显著的性能提升，但由于冗余推理（即“过度思考”）而导致效率低下。现有的缓解这一问题的方法要么依赖于静态难度估计，要么需要任务特定的训练，因此无法适应推理过程中动态变化的复杂性。在这项工作中，我们经验性地证明，问题难度在推理过程中动态演变，并线性编码在LRM的步骤级嵌入中。基于这一见解，我们提出了DyCon，一个无需训练的框架，利用潜在步骤级表示来显式建模不断演变的任务难度，从而实现对推理深度的动态控制以缓解过度思考问题。在四个模型（从4B到32B参数）以及数学推理、通用问答和编程任务等十二个基准上进行的广泛实验表明，DyCon通过减少冗余步骤显著提高了推理效率，同时不牺牲准确性或泛化能力。代码可在https://github.com/yu-lin-li/DyCon获取。

Original abstract: Recent advances in Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) demonstrate remarkable performance improvements by iteratively reflecting, exploring, and executing complex tasks, yet suffer from inefficiencies due to redundant reasoning, known as "overthinking". Existing methods to mitigate this issue either rely on static difficulty estimates or require task-specific training, and thus fail to adapt to the dynamic complexity during reasoning. In this work, we empirically show that the problem difficulty evolves dynamically throughout the reasoning process and is linearly encoded in the LRM's step-level embeddings. Building on this insight, we propose DyCon, a training-free framework that leverages latent step-level representations to explicitly model the evolving task difficulty, enabling the dynamic control of reasoning depth to mitigate the overthinking issue. Extensive experiments conducted on four models ranging from 4B to 32B, and across twelve benchmarks in math reasoning, general question answering, and coding tasks demonstrate that DyCon significantly enhances reasoning efficiency by reducing redundant steps without sacrificing accuracy or generalization. Code is available at https://github.com/yu-lin-li/DyCon.

</details>


### [33] [Think Fast: Estimating No-CoT Task-Completion Time Horizons of Frontier AI Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07157v3)
*Dewi Gould,Francis Rhys Ward,Anders Cairns Woodruff,Rauno Arike,Josh Hills,Alex Serrano,Ida Caspary,Jason Ross Brown,Jo J. Jiao,Patrick Leask,Twm Stone,Ram Potham,Ionut Gabriel Stan,Harry Mayne,Simeon Hellsten,Shubhorup Biswas,Ariana Azarbal,William L. Anderson,Elle Najt,Ryan Greenblatt,Julian Stastny*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 评估无CoT推理能力，对agent是否依赖显式推理有参考价值。

TL;DR: 前沿AI模型在没有思维链推理的情况下，其能力每约一年翻一番，预计到2030年无CoT的50%任务完成时间将超过25分钟，威胁现有安全监控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 监控思维链推理是当前确保AI安全的关键手段，但模型可能发展出无需外部推理标记的内部推理能力，从而规避监督。需要量化这种风险。

Method: 构建包含30,000+问题和43个基准的测试集，估计50%任务完成时间范围（TH）和50%推理标记范围，比较模型与人类能力。

Result: 无CoT的50% TH每六年翻一番，GPT-5.5达3分钟，推理标记超1500；预测2028年超7分钟，2030年超25分钟。

Conclusion: 前沿模型无CoT推理能力快速增长，可能削弱基于CoT的安全措施，建议开发者明确跟踪该趋势。

中文摘要：为了确保前沿AI模型的安全，许多努力依赖于监控它们的思维链（CoT）推理。如果模型能够在不使用显式思维标记的情况下进行足够复杂的内部推理，这将破坏这种监督。我们在超过30,000个问题的测试集上测量了前沿模型在没有CoT情况下的推理能力，这些测试涵盖43个基准，包括数学、编码、谜题、因果关系、心理理论和战略推理领域。为了与人类进行比较，我们估计了50%任务完成时间范围（TH）：人类完成模型以50%成功率解决的任务所需的时间。我们还补充了一个50%推理标记范围：模型以50%成功率解决问题所需的o3-mini推理标记的最小数量。我们发现，前沿模型的无CoT 50% TH在过去六年中大约每年翻一番，GPT-5.5的TH超过3分钟，推理标记范围超过1500个标记。我们的中位数估计预测，前沿模型的无CoT TH可能在2028年超过7分钟，到2030年超过25分钟，尽管这些预测具有很大的不确定性。我们建议前沿开发者明确跟踪这一指标。

Original abstract: Many efforts to ensure frontier AI models are safe rely on monitoring their chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning. If models become able to perform sufficiently complex reasoning internally, without explicit thinking tokens, this would undermine such oversight. We measure how well frontier models reason without CoT across a suite of over 30,000 questions spanning 43 benchmarks in domains including math, coding, puzzles, causality, theory-of-mind, and strategic reasoning. To compare models against humans, we estimate the $50\%$-task-completion time horizon (TH): the human time required for tasks a model completes with $50\%$ success rate. We complement this with a $50\%$ reasoning token horizon: the minimum number of o3-mini reasoning tokens needed for tasks a model solves with $50\%$ success rate. We find that the no-CoT $50\%$ TH of frontier models has been doubling roughly every year over the past six years, with GPT-5.5's TH reaching over 3 minutes and reasoning token horizon exceeding 1,500 tokens. Our median estimates predict that frontier no-CoT THs could exceed 7 minutes by 2028, and 25 minutes by 2030, though these projections carry substantial uncertainty. We recommend frontier developers track this explicitly.
