### [64] [What Your Posts Reveal: A Benchmark and Agentic Framework for User-Level Privacy Leakage on Social Media](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06784v1)
*Zifan Peng,Yini Huang,Aiwen Lu,Qiming Ye,Peixian Zhang,Jingyi Zheng,Yule Liu,Xuechao Wang,Xinlei He,Jiaheng Wei*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 提出社交隐私泄露推断的agent框架，使用溯因推理和跨帖子聚合，属于通用agent推理方法。

TL;DR: 提出SopriBench基准和PES指标，以及Argus框架，用于检测社交媒体中累积的多模态隐私泄露，效果提升25%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏统一的用户级多模态隐私泄露基准和能够衡量暴露严重程度的评估指标。

Method: 基于真实语料抽象泄露模式构建合成基准SopriBench，提出隐私暴露分数PES，设计基于溯因推理的无需训练代理框架Argus。

Result: Argus达到0.55 PES，比最强基线提升25%，在跨帖子泄露上提升最大。

Conclusion: 有效评估了累积隐私泄露，Argus框架在隐私推断上性能优越。

中文摘要：社交媒体的公开帖子可以通过分散在文本、图像或元数据中的微弱线索泄露私人信息。这种泄露通常是累积性和跨帖子的：单独看来无害的线索可能共同暴露用户的家庭、工作地点或日常行程。然而，当前的研究缺乏一个统一的用户级多模态隐私泄露基准，以及一个能够捕捉超出二元准确性的暴露严重程度的评估指标。为了填补这些空白，我们提出了SopriBench，这是一个合成基准，其泄露模式是从Rednote和Instagram账户的私人参考语料库中抽象出来的，涵盖50个用户画像和1569张图像，包含属性、上下文敏感性、粒度、泄露类型、推理难度和支持性证据。我们进一步引入了隐私暴露分数（PES），它通过上下文敏感性加权值粒度。受溯因推理的启发，我们提出了Argus，一个无需训练的代理框架，用于累积性泄露推理。Argus从累积的证据中形成假设，验证支持性证据，并将跨帖子的线索聚合到隐私画像中，实现了0.55的PES，比最强的基线提高了25%，其中最大的提升来自跨帖子泄露。

Original abstract: Public social media posts can reveal private information through weak cues scattered across text, images, or metadata. Such leakage is often cumulative and cross-post: cues that appear harmless in isolation may jointly expose a user's home, workplace, or routine. However, current research lacks a unified benchmark for user-level multimodal privacy leakage and an evaluation metric that captures exposure severity beyond binary accuracy.
  To address these gaps, we propose SopriBench, a synthetic benchmark guided by leakage patterns abstracted from a private reference corpus of Rednote and Instagram accounts, covering 50 user profiles and 1,569 images with attributes, contextual sensitivity, granularity, leakage type, inference difficulty, and supporting evidence. We further introduce the Privacy Exposure Score (PES), which weights value granularity by contextual sensitivity. Inspired by abductive reasoning, we introduce Argus, a training-free agentic framework for cumulative leakage inference. Argus forms hypotheses from accumulated evidence, verifies supporting evidence, and aggregates cross-post cues into privacy profiles, achieving 0.55 PES, a 25% improvement over the strongest baseline, with the largest gain on cross-post leakage.

</details>


### [65] [MLingualFC: Evaluating Jailbreak Vulnerabilities in Multilingual Vision-Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07706v1)
*Rishabh Makwana,Mamta,Deeksha Varshney,Oana Cocarascu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 多语言VLM安全性评估，对agent安全测试有参考

TL;DR: 提出了MLingualFC多语言多模态基准，评估VLM在流程图越狱下的安全性，发现拉丁字母语言攻击成功率高，非拉丁字母语言成功率低，表明安全机制跨语言泛化不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLM安全研究多局限于英语，缺乏多语言场景下结构化视觉提示（如流程图）越狱攻击的系统评估。

Method: 构建MLingualFC基准，将有害指令编码为五种语言的流程图图像，并在黑盒设置下评估Qwen2.5-VL、Gemma-4、Pangea等VLM的攻击成功率。

Result: 拉丁字母语言（西班牙语、罗马尼亚语、德语）攻击成功率高，非拉丁字母语言（旁遮普语）成功率低，印地语居中；视觉编码有效绕过安全对齐。

Conclusion: 当前VLM安全机制无法跨语言和模态泛化，需要针对多语言场景设计更鲁棒的安全对齐方法。

中文摘要：视觉语言模型（VLM）在多模态任务中表现出强大的性能，但其安全鲁棒性仍然是一个开放挑战。虽然先前的工作表明流程图等结构化视觉提示可以有效越狱VLM，但现有研究主要局限于英语中心设置。在本文中，我们引入了MLingualFC，这是一个多语言多模态基准，旨在使用结构化流程图表示评估VLM在不同语言下的越狱漏洞。MLingualFC将有害指令编码为五种语言（印地语、旁遮普语、西班牙语、罗马尼亚语和德语）的流程图图像。我们在黑盒威胁模型下评估了最先进的多语言VLM，包括Qwen2.5-VL、Gemma-4和Pangea。我们的结果揭示了显著的多语言安全差距。基于流程图的攻击在拉丁字母语言中实现了高攻击成功率（ASR），表明有害内容的视觉编码有效绕过了跨语言的安全对齐。相比之下，非拉丁字母语言（如旁遮普语）的ASR显著较低，表明潜在的视觉文本识别限制而非更强的安全对齐。这些发现突显了当前VLM安全机制无法跨语言和模态泛化。资源可在https://github.com/Rishabhpm23/MLingualFC获取。

Original abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have demonstrated strong performance across multimodal tasks, yet their safety robustness remains an open challenge. While prior work has shown that structured visual prompts such as flowcharts can effectively jailbreak VLMs, existing studies are largely limited to English-centric settings. In this paper, we introduce MLingualFC, a multilingual multimodal benchmark designed to evaluate jailbreak vulnerabilities of VLMs across diverse languages using structured flowchart representations. MLingualFC encodes harmful instructions into flowchart images across five languages (Hindi, Punjabi, Spanish, Romanian, and German). We evaluate state-of-the-art multilingual VLMs, including Qwen2.5-VL, Gemma-4, and Pangea, under a black-box threat model. Our results reveal significant multilingual safety gaps. Flowchart-based attacks achieve high attack success rates (ASR) in case of Latin script languages, demonstrating that visual encoding of harmful content effectively bypasses safety alignment across languages. In contrast, non-Latin script languages such as Punjabi exhibit substantially lower ASR, suggesting potential limitations in visual text recognition rather than stronger safety alignment. These findings highlight that current VLM safety mechanisms fail to generalize across languages and modalities. Resources are available at https://github.com/Rishabhpm23/MLingualFC

</details>


### [66] [MalSkillBench: A Runtime-Verified Benchmark of Malicious Agent Skills](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07131v3)
*Wenbo Guo,Wei Zeng,Chengwei Liu,Xiaojun Jia,Yijia Xu,Lei Tang,Yong Fang,Yang Liu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了MalSkillBench，首个运行时验证的恶意AI助手技能基准，包含3,944个恶意技能和4,000个良性技能，测量发现现有检测器在混合性威胁上表现不均衡，需联合推理代码和指令。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检测工具从未在覆盖代码和指令混合空间的已验证真值上进行衡量，导致其有效性未知且野外评估有偏。

Method: 构建MalSkillBench：通过闭环生成-验证-反馈流水线产生3,214个恶意技能（在Docker沙箱中验证），添加703个野外恶意技能和4,000个良性技能，按三维分类法标注，并评估多种检测器。

Result: 代码注入验证成功率94.5%，提示注入仅75.8%；野外样本偏窄（86.6%为单一行为）；最强检测器在代码注入上召回率98.4%，但在提示注入和助手控制攻击上表现差；仅野外评估使排名波动高达66个召回点。

Conclusion: 检测恶意技能需要联合推理任务意图、代码和指令，现有工具无法完整覆盖该混合空间。

中文摘要：AI编码助手（如Claude Code和Gemini CLI）日益通过第三方技能扩展自身：这些技能是包含自然语言指令、可执行脚本和工具权限的markdown包。由于技能同时包含代码和面向助手的指令，它引入了一种供应链依赖，其风险既非纯代码也非纯提示。检测工具从未针对覆盖这种混合空间的已验证真值进行衡量，导致其有效性未知，且仅基于野外样本的评估存在偏差。我们提出MalSkillBench，首个运行时验证的恶意助手技能基准：包含3,944个恶意技能，按照108个单元格的三维分类法进行标注。其中，3,214个来自闭环生成-验证-反馈流水线，仅接受在系统调用监控和LLM裁判下于Docker沙箱内触发恶意行为的样本；我们添加了703个野外样本和4,000个匹配的良性技能。我们的测量结果一致：代码注入的验证成功率达到94.5%，但提示注入仅为75.8%，这种脆弱性后来也使其难以检测；野外样本范围狭窄，由一次加密货币盗窃活动主导（86.6%为单一行为，81%来自两个账户），此外还有一小部分但架构新颖的尾部攻击针对助手控制平面；最强的技能专用检测器在代码注入上达到98.4%的召回率，但在提示注入和助手控制攻击上表现崩溃，仅基于野外样本的评分使排名波动高达66个召回点；供应链扫描器和提示注入防御各自仅看到技能的一半，且任何组合都无法恢复代码-指令关系。因此，检测恶意技能需要联合推理任务意图、代码和指令。我们发布了数据集、流水线、基线和结果。

Original abstract: AI coding agents such as Claude Code and Gemini CLI increasingly extend themselves with third-party skills: markdown packages bundling natural-language instructions, executable scripts, and tool permissions. Because a skill is at once code and agent-facing instruction, it introduces a supply chain dependency whose risk is neither pure code nor pure prompt. Detection tools have never been measured against verified ground truth spanning this hybrid space, leaving their effectiveness unknown and wild-only evaluations biased.
  We present MalSkillBench, the first runtime-verified benchmark of malicious agent skills: 3,944 malicious skills labeled along a three-dimensional taxonomy of 108 cells. Of these, 3,214 come from a closed-loop Generate-Verify-Feedback pipeline admitting only samples whose malicious behavior fires inside a Docker sandbox under system-call monitoring and an LLM judge; we add 703 in-the-wild and 4,000 matched benign skills. Our measurements are consistent: code injection reaches 94.5% verification yield but prompt injection only 75.8%, the same fragility that later makes it hard to detect; the wild sample is narrow, dominated by one cryptocurrency-theft campaign (86.6% one behavior, 81% from two accounts) with a small but architecturally new tail attacking the agent control plane; the strongest skill-specific detector reaches 98.4% recall on code injection yet collapses on prompt-injection and agent-control attacks, and wild-only scoring swings the ranking by up to 66 recall points; supply-chain scanners and prompt-injection defenses each see only half of a skill, and no combination recovers the code-instruction relationship. Detecting malicious skills therefore requires reasoning jointly over task intent, code, and instructions. We release the dataset, pipeline, baselines, and results.

</details>


### [67] [From Privacy to Workflow Integrity: Communication-Graph Metadata in Autonomous Agent Interoperability](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07150v3)
*Bijaya Dangol*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 研究agent互操作中的通信图元数据威胁，涉及agent安全与隐私，可迁移到coding agent。

TL;DR: 本文揭示智能体通信协议中元数据泄露导致工作流完整性威胁，提出防御属性并实验验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有协议保护内容但暴露通信图，在智能体系统中该图可被利用破坏工作流完整性，而不仅是隐私。

Method: 提出通信图威胁模型，定义传输层和引导层隐私属性及不可区分博弈语义，在真实A2A流量上使用标签盲分类器和防御感知对手进行实验评估。

Result: 标签盲分类器从被动元数据中6倍随机概率恢复任务类别（仅开头），防御感知对手无法完全消除，完整性和隐私在防御下分离。

Conclusion: 需要元数据保护以维护工作流完整性，现有传输协议不足，提出的属性框架可指导防御。

中文摘要：Agent互操作性协议（如A2A和MCP）标准化了智能体之间的通信内容，但假设基于地址的传输。无论是通过HTTP(S)还是通过基于MLS的SLIM等内容保护绑定，这些传输都保护了消息内容，却暴露了通信图：哪个智能体联系哪个、何时以及频率。在智能体系统中，这个图比隐私框架所暗示的更加重要。端点带有能力标签，工作流是结构化且链式的，交互与动作耦合，因此观察者恢复的不仅仅是过去的关系：它可以从一个重复出现的待定工作流的开头识别它，并以机器速度在其完成之前采取行动。威胁在于工作流完整性，而不仅仅是隐私。我们提出了一个关于通信图的威胁模型，并找出了其元数据之所以具有显著后果的原因：不是更强的指纹识别，而是跨独立信任域的暴露，与自主行动相结合。我们定义了传输层和引导层的隐私属性，赋予它们不可区分博弈语义，评估了各种传输，并给出了一个A2A案例研究，其中元数据保护绑定暴露了其隐式的身份假设。在来自官方参考智能体的真实多智能体A2A流量语料库上，在一个实时的A2A绑定上，并使用生成模型作为受控工具，一个标签盲分类器从被动元数据中以6倍随机概率恢复任务类别，仅从开头就能做到；一个防御感知的对手无法推翻这一点，只有完整的属性集才能使恢复趋近随机概率。对泄露采取行动与可恢复性不同：在固定预算下，对手在语料库上获得了千里眼攻击者优势的0.63（0.41来自工作流开头），由顶级精度而非整体准确率决定，因此在防御下完整性和隐私发生了分离。

Original abstract: Agent-interoperability protocols such as A2A and MCP standardize what agents say to one another but assume address-based transport. Whether over HTTP(S) or a content-protecting binding such as MLS-based SLIM, these transports protect message content yet leave the communication graph exposed: which agent contacts which, when, and how often. In agent systems this graph is more consequential than a privacy framing suggests. Endpoints are capability-labeled, workflows are structured and chained, and interactions are coupled to actions, so an observer recovers more than past relationships: it can recognize a recurring pending workflow from its opening and, at machine speed, act on it before it completes. The threat is one of workflow integrity, not privacy alone. We give a threat model for the communication graph and locate what makes its metadata distinctively consequential: not stronger fingerprinting but exposure across independent trust domains, coupled to autonomous action. We define transport- and bootstrap-layer privacy properties, give them an indistinguishability-game semantics, evaluate transports, and give an A2A case study where a metadata-protecting binding surfaces its implicit identity assumptions. On a corpus of real multi-agent A2A traffic from the official reference agents, on a live A2A binding, and with a generative model as a controlled instrument, a label-blind classifier recovers a task's class from passive metadata at 6x chance, and from only its opening; a defense-aware adversary does not overturn this, and only the full set of properties drives recovery toward chance. Acting on the leak is distinct from recoverability: under a fixed budget an adversary captures 0.63 of a clairvoyant attacker's advantage on the corpus (0.41 from a workflow's opening), governed by top-ranked precision rather than overall accuracy, so integrity and privacy come apart under defense.

</details>


### [68] [On the Shoulders of Giants: Empowering Automated Smart Contract Auditing via the GiAnt Corpus](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07363v1)
*Xiaoting Zhang,Zhipeng Gao,Yiran Lv,Xing Hu,Feifei Niu,Xin Xia*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出GiANT框架，从真实审计报告中自动构建高质量智能合约漏洞数据集，生成包含7,711个漏洞的GiAnt语料库，经人工评估质量极高，并基准测试了4个LLM以验证实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能合约审计数据集存在人工扩展瓶颈和粒度、多样性不足的问题，需要自动化的高质量数据集构建方法。

Method: 采用分治策略和思维链技术从Code4rena报告提取结构化漏洞信息，并通过LLM作为评判机制进行质量保证。

Result: 在388份报告上生成7,711个漏洞发现，人工评估质量得分4.76±0.37，评估者间一致性κ=0.88；基准测试4个LLM建立性能基线。

Conclusion: GiANT能有效自动构建高质量数据集，为智能合约安全研究提供数据基础，有助于未来自动化审计研究。

中文摘要：高质量的智能合约审计数据集对于评估安全工具和推进智能合约安全研究至关重要。现有数据集的两个主要局限是人工导致的扩展瓶颈以及数据粒度和多样性的不足。为解决这些局限，我们提出了GiANT，一个自动化框架，旨在通过从现实世界的审计报告中提炼漏洞洞察来整理智能合约审计数据集。GiANT采用分治策略结合思维链技术，从Code4rena报告中提取结构化漏洞信息，随后通过LLM作为评判机制进行严格的质量保证。为评估GiANT的有效性，我们将其应用于388份真实审计报告，生成了包含五个严重级别共7,711个漏洞发现的GiAnt语料库。对数据集的人工评估展示了信息提取的卓越可靠性，平均质量得分为4.76±0.37（满分5分），评估者间一致性κ为0.88。我们进一步通过基准测试4个最先进的LLM在漏洞检测、代码摘要、缓解建议和自动Gas优化任务上的表现，验证了该数据集的实用性，建立了性能基线，从而为未来自动智能合约审计研究提供了宝贵的数据基础。

Original abstract: High-quality smart contract auditing datasets are crucial for evaluating security tools and advancing smart contract security research. Two major limitations of existing datasets are the manual-induced scalability bottleneck and the deficiency in data granularity and diversity. To address these limitations, we propose GiANT, an automated framework designed to curate smart contract auditing datasets by distilling vulnerability insights from real-world auditing reports. GiANT employs a divide-and-conquer strategy coupled with the Chain-of-Thought technique to extract structured vulnerability information from Code4rena reports, followed by an LLM-as-a-judge mechanism to perform rigorous quality assurance. To evaluate GiANT's effectiveness, we run it on 388 real-world audit reports and generate the GiAnt Corpus comprising 7,711 vulnerability findings across five severity levels. Manual assessment of the dataset demonstrates exceptional reliability in information extraction, achieving a mean quality score of $4.76\pm0.37$ (out of 5) with inter-rater agreement $κ$ of 0.88. We further validate the practicality of our dataset by benchmarking 4 state-of-the-art LLMs on vulnerability detection, code summarization, mitigation recommendation, and automated gas optimization tasks, to establish performance baselines, thereby providing a valuable data foundation for future research in automated smart contract auditing.

</details>


### [69] [MOLOT System Card: Malicious Operational Logic Observation Transformer](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07792v1)
*Daniil Lopatkin,Maksim Mitrofanov,Stanislav Rakovsky,Aleksandr Khalikov*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将源代码表示为从静态调用图派生的行为序列，构建模型进行检测，并设计解释阶段将可疑行为映射回代码位置。

Result: 在Python和JavaScript包上评估，与开源工具相比，在运行时、内存和误报率等产品约束下表现良好，同时发布了开源基准数据集Open Malicious-Code Bench。

中文摘要：MOLOT（恶意操作逻辑观察变换器）是一个静态恶意代码检测系统，专为静态应用安全测试（SAST）场景设计，在该场景下包元数据、维护者历史记录和动态执行轨迹可能不可用或不可靠。该系统将源代码表示为从静态调用图派生的行为序列，并包含一个解释阶段，该阶段对可疑行为活动进行排序并将其映射回源代码位置。该方法在来自PyPI和npm的Python和JavaScript包上进行了评估，与开源检测工具进行了比较，并在实际审核工作流中观察到的运行时、内存使用和误报率等产品约束条件下进行了验证。我们还发布了Open Malicious-Code Bench，一个用于可重复评估恶意包检测方法的公共基准。结果表明，静态行为序列建模可以为现代DevSecOps工作流提供准确、可解释且可部署的恶意代码检测。

Original abstract: MOLOT (Malicious Operational Logic Observation Transformer) is a static malicious-code detection system designed for SAST setup where package metadata, maintainer history, and dynamic execution traces may be unavailable or unreliable. The system represents source code as behavior sequences derived from static call graphs, includes an explanation stage that ranks suspicious behavior activities and maps them back to source-code locations. The approach is evaluated on Python and JavaScript packages from PyPI and npm, compared with opensource detection tools, and validated under product constraints including runtime, memory use, and false-positive rates observed in a real moderation workflow. We also release Open Malicious-Code Bench, a public benchmark for reproducible evaluation of malicious-package detection methods. The results show that static behavior-sequence modeling can provide accurate, explainable, and deployable malicious-code detection for modern DevSecOps workflows.

### [70] [Beyond Pass/Fail: Using Process Mining to Understand How LLMs Resist (and Fail) Red Team Attacks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07833v1)
*Zvi Topol*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 过程挖掘分析LLM红队攻击防御，对agent安全性与行为分析有价值

TL;DR: 提出将过程挖掘用于分析红队追踪的序列行为，揭示LLM防御结构差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准红队评估仅用ASR单一指标，忽略攻击的序列结构，无法全面反映模型防御行为。

Method: 进行受控实验，使用HarmBench提示和多种变异策略，从事件日志提取DFG和状态转移矩阵。

Result: 发现GPT-OSS和Llama具有不同的防御结构，mutator有效性不对称，越狱时间分布差异大。

Conclusion: 过程挖掘能揭示ASR无法捕获的防御轮廓，为红队评估提供更丰富的洞察。

中文摘要：标准AI红队评估将对抗性活动简化为单一的二元结果，即攻击成功率（ASR），而没有考虑模型抵抗或屈服于攻击的顺序结构。我们提出将过程挖掘（一种从事件日志中发现和分析过程模型的学科）应用于红队追踪。我们进行了一项受控实验，使用60个HarmBench提示对抗两个LLM：GPT-OSS 120B和Llama 3.3 70B，使用10种提示变异策略，每个提示最多尝试110次。从得到的8,575个评分事件中，我们提取了直接跟随图（DFGs）和状态转移矩阵，这些揭示了仅凭ASR无法发现的结构性不同的防御轮廓：GPT-OSS表现出接近吸收的拒绝状态，而Llama则呈现多条从拒绝到成功越狱的多孔逃生路线。我们进一步表明，变异器的有效性在模型间是不对称的，并且越狱时间分布相差一个数量级。

Original abstract: Standard AI red teaming evaluations reduce adversarial campaigns to a single binary outcome, attack success rate (ASR), not taking into account the sequential structure of how models resist or yield to attacks. We propose applying process mining, a discipline for discovering and analyzing process models from event logs, to red teaming traces. We conduct a controlled experiment pitting 60 HarmBench prompts against two LLMs, GPT-OSS 120B and Llama 3.3 70B, using 10 prompt mutation strategies over up to 110 attempts per prompt. From the resulting 8,575 scored events we extract Directly-Follows Graphs (DFGs) and state transition matrices that reveal structurally distinct defense profiles invisible to ASR alone: GPT-OSS exhibits a near-absorbing refusal state, while Llama presents multiple porous escape routes from refusal to getting successfully jailbroken. We further show that mutator effectiveness is asymmetric across models and that time-to-jailbreak distributions differ by an order of magnitude.

### [71] [Mitigating Anchoring Bias in LLM-Based Agents for Energy-Efficient 6G Autonomous Networks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18272v2)
*Hatim Chergui,Claudia Carballo González,Farhad Rezazadeh,Merouane Debbah*

Main category: cs.NI

Selection reason: LLM agent在6G网络中的锚定偏见缓解策略，方法可迁移到coding agent。

TL;DR: A framework using LLM agents for 6G network slicing mitigates anchoring bias via Weibull-distributed randomization, achieving up to 25% energy savings with sub-second inference.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM agents suffer from anchoring bias causing network over-provisioning; need for cognitive debiasing in autonomous resource negotiation.

Method: Proposes randomized anchoring strategy with Truncated 3-Parameter Weibull distribution, integrated with CVaR-based Digital Twins; proves Bimodal Constraint-Avoidance Utility Theorem.

Result: Empirical validation on 1B-parameter model shows dual-regime bounds; de-biasing achieves 25% energy savings and sub-second inference (0.95s mean).

Conclusion: The lightweight LLM-based multi-agent framework is feasible for O-RAN non-RT RIC timescales, enabling zero-touch network slicing with SLA guarantees.

中文摘要：本文提出了一种自主智能体资源协商框架，旨在利用大型语言模型（LLM）智能体实现6G架构中的零接触网络切片。虽然LLM提供了强大的推理能力，但我们证明此类智能体固有地受到锚定偏差的影响，僵化地坚持初始启发式提案，导致严重的网络过度配置。为了系统地缓解这种认知偏差，我们提出了一种新颖的随机锚定策略，通过截断三参数威布尔分布建模。这种数学上有界的方法与采用条件风险价值（CVaR）的突发感知数字孪生（DT）无缝集成，以严格保证严格的服务水平协议（SLA）尾部延迟。为了验证我们的方法，我们引入并证明了双峰约束避免效用定理，表明虽然可行的协商遵循经典凸界，但高度约束的场景会经历由逆有理衰减包络控制的相变。使用本地托管的10亿参数模型otel-llm-1b-it生成的经验结果证实了这些双区域边界。我们的认知去偏成功打破了僵化的协商模式，迫使智能体主动探索以安全地利用SLA边界，并将系统节能提升高达25%。关键的是，轻量级的10亿LLM实现了亚秒级推理延迟（平均0.95秒），确保我们的多智能体框架与O-RAN非实时RAN智能控制器（non-RT RIC）的操作时间尺度兼容。我们的源代码可在https://github.com/HatimChergui上用于非商业用途。

Original abstract: This paper presents an autonomous agentic resource negotiation framework designed to enable zero-touch network slicing in 6G architectures using Large Language Model (LLM) agents. While LLMs offer powerful reasoning capabilities, we demonstrate that such agents inherently suffer from anchoring bias, rigidly adhering to initial heuristic proposals and causing severe network over-provisioning. To systematically mitigate this cognitive bias, we propose a novel randomized anchoring strategy modeled via a Truncated 3-Parameter Weibull distribution. This mathematically bounded approach seamlessly integrates with burst-aware Digital Twins (DTs) employing Conditional Value at Risk (CVaR) to rigorously guarantee strict Service Level Agreement (SLA) tail-latencies. To validate our methodology, we introduce and prove the \emph{Bimodal Constraint-Avoidance Utility Theorem}, demonstrating that while feasible negotiations follow classical convex bounds, highly constrained scenarios undergo a phase transition governed by an inverse rational decay envelope. Empirical results generated using a locally hosted 1B-parameter model otel-llm-1b-it confirm these dual-regime bounds. Our cognitive de-biasing successfully dismantles rigid negotiation patterns, forcing agents into active exploration to safely ride SLA boundaries and boost system energy savings up to 25\%. Crucially, the lightweight 1B LLM achieves sub-second inference latencies (0.95s mean), ensuring our multi-agent framework is compatible with the operational timescales of the O-RAN non-Real-Time RAN Intelligent Controller (non-RT RIC)\footnote{Our source code is available for non-commercial use at https://github.com/HatimChergui.

</details>

Original abstract: High-performance computing (HPC) clusters remain the backbone of large-scale scientific computation, traditionally executing deterministic, linear pipelines optimised for predictable performance. However, the pervasive integration of artificial intelligence (AI) and foundation models into scientific research has introduced a fundamentally new computational paradigm. AI-driven workflows are characteristically iterative, data-driven, and probabilistic, introducing unique challenges regarding data gravity, heterogeneous resource management, and complex workflow orchestration.
  This guide provides twelve practical tips designed to help researchers design efficient, scalable, and reproducible AI-driven HPC workflows. By addressing critical system-level bottlenecks - such as containerisation for environment portability, strategic deployment of job arrays, explicit feedback loop mechanics, and I/O optimisation for small files - this article offers a framework for transitioning from rigid execution pipelines to adaptive, intelligent computational environments. While these architectural principles are broadly applicable across distributed environments, they are particularly tailored to the resource-intensive throughput demands of modern computational biology.

### [73] [Cost-Aware Speculative Execution for LLM-Agent Workflows: An Integrated Five-Dimension Method](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07846v1)
*Faisal Fareed*

Main category: cs.DC

Selection reason: 成本感知推测执行框架，直接优化LLM-agent工作流效率，高度相关

TL;DR: 通过五个设计决策和贝叶斯估计的推测执行方法，在LLM-agent工作流中平衡延迟与成本，并经过校准和验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 减少LLM-agent工作流中因等待上下游操作产生的空闲时间，同时管理推测执行带来的真实货币成本和不确定性。

Method: 围绕五个设计决策（D1-D5）组织方法，包括贝叶斯Beta-Binomial后验概率估计、期望值决策规则，以及运行时机制、五阶段校准流水线和负载适配准则。

Result: 合成验证确认了决策边界、概率阈值、后验恢复和流取消行为，与四个系统的对比显示了差异。

Conclusion: 该方法能有效管理推测执行在成本与延迟之间的权衡，并通过校准和验证确保鲁棒性。

中文摘要：LLM-agent工作流将模型调用和工具调用串联起来，并且大部分挂钟时间都花在等待上游操作完成，然后下游操作才能开始。推测执行可以通过使用预测的上游输入启动下游操作来回收空闲时间，但在这里每次推测都会花费真实货币（按令牌计费），且其成功概率难以估计并随时间漂移。本文提出了一种围绕五个设计决策组织的方法：（D1）在上游完成之前启动下游操作；（D2）以真实美元按输入和输出分别定价每次推测；（D3）暴露一个单一的调节旋钮来控制延迟与成本；（D4）通过一个期望值规则进行决策，该规则包含一个失败加权的成本项和一个偏好调整的阈值；（D5）使用贝叶斯Beta-Binomial后验估计成功概率，其先验根据依赖类型分类法确定。这些想法的变体出现在最近的工作中；其组合，以及每次决策都以美元记录，是本文的新颖之处。该规则仅触发通过可接受性前提条件的边（无副作用、幂等或可在提交屏障后阶段化），因为错误的推测通过重新执行回滚，这会退还令牌但无法撤销不可逆的副作用。我们指定了运行时机制、一个闭式结果（表明随着上游分支因子增长，规则会自我限制）、一个五阶段校准流水线（离线重放、影子、金丝雀、在线校准、漂移触发的紧急停止开关），以及一个涵盖八个生产原型的负载适配准则。与四个最接近的已发表系统（DSP、Speculative Actions v2、Sherlock、B-PASTE）的对比表显示了每个维度上的差异点，合成验证套件确认了预测的决策边界、概率阈值、后验恢复和流取消行为。

Original abstract: LLM-agent workflows chain model calls and tool invocations, and spend most of their wall-clock time waiting on upstream operations before downstream ones can start. Speculative execution can reclaim that idle time by launching a downstream operation with a predicted upstream input, but here each speculation costs real money (per-token billing) and its success probability is hard to estimate and drifts over time. This paper presents a method organized around five design decisions: (D1) start a downstream operation before its upstream completes; (D2) price each speculation in real dollars at separate input and output rates; (D3) expose a single operator dial for latency versus cost; (D4) decide via an expected-value rule with a failure-weighted cost term and a preference-adjusted threshold; and (D5) estimate the success probability with a Bayesian Beta-Binomial posterior whose prior is keyed to a dependency-type taxonomy. Variants of these ideas appear in recent work; the combination, with every decision logged in dollars, is what is new. The rule fires only on edges passing an admissibility precondition (side-effect-free, idempotent, or stageable behind a commit barrier), since a wrong speculation is rolled back by re-execution, which refunds tokens but cannot un-send an irreversible side effect. We specify the runtime mechanics, a closed-form result that the rule self-limits as the upstream branching factor grows, a five-stage calibration pipeline (offline replay, shadow, canary, online calibration, drift-triggered kill-switch), and a workload-fit rubric over eight production archetypes. Contrast tables against the four closest published systems (DSP, Speculative Actions v2, Sherlock, B-PASTE) show differentiators on every dimension, and a synthetic validation suite confirms the predicted decision boundary, probability threshold, posterior recovery, and streaming-cancellation behavior.

</details>

# cs.CL [[Back]](#toc)

### [74] [Progress-SQL: Improving Reinforcement Learning for Text-to-SQL via Progressive Rewards](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06825v1)
*Shihao Zhang,Xiaoman Wang,Yuan Liu,Yunshi Lan,Weining Qian*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多轮RL框架用于Text-to-SQL，使用渐进奖励和诊断树，属于代码生成agent的迭代改进。

TL;DR: 提出了Progress-SQL，一种带有渐进奖励的多轮强化学习框架，通过Oracle引导的诊断树提供结构对齐和反馈，结合多种奖励信号，显著提升了Text-to-SQL性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习方法优化基于单个SQL状态的一次性奖励，无法有效引导多轮SQL修正，且难以捕捉逐步改进。

Method: 提出Progress-SQL框架，包括Oracle引导的诊断树（ODT）抽象SQL子句结构并生成反馈，定义渐进奖励（结合结构对齐和词汇对齐）、渐进延迟奖励和执行状态奖励。

Result: 在BIRD、Spider及其鲁棒性变体上实验，方法在主要和鲁棒性评估中持续提升Text-to-SQL性能。

Conclusion: Progress-SQL通过多轮强化学习与渐进奖励有效提升了Text-to-SQL的生成质量，尤其在多轮修正和鲁棒性方面表现优越。

中文摘要：强化学习近期在提升大型语言模型用于Text-to-SQL生成方面显示出潜力，但现有方法通常优化基于单个SQL状态定义的一次性奖励。这种奖励为迭代式SQL修正提供的指导有限，并且不足以捕捉多轮SQL改进的提升。本文提出Progress-SQL，一种带有渐进奖励的多轮强化学习框架用于Text-to-SQL。我们的方法引入了一个Oracle引导的诊断树（ODT），它将SQL查询抽象为子句级别的结构轮廓，并为下一轮改进生成诊断反馈。为了提供密集且鲁棒的奖励信号，我们将基于ODT的结构对齐与词汇对齐相结合，并定义一个渐进奖励来衡量从初始SQL到最终SQL的改进。我们进一步结合了一个优先正确性的渐进延迟奖励和一个鼓励从无效SQL中恢复的执行状态奖励。在BIRD、Spider和Spider鲁棒性变体上的实验表明，我们的方法在主要评估和鲁棒性评估上均持续提升了Text-to-SQL性能。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning has recently shown promise in improving large language models for Text-to-SQL generation, yet existing methods typically optimize one-shot rewards defined over a single SQL state. Such rewards provide limited guidance for iterative SQL correction and are insufficient to capture the improvement of multi-turn SQL refinement. In this paper, we propose Progress-SQL, a multi-turn reinforcement learning framework with progressive rewards for Text-to-SQL. Our approach introduces an Oracle-guided Diagnostic Tree (ODT), which abstracts SQL queries into clause-level structural profiles and produces diagnostic feedback for next-turn refinement. To provide dense and robust reward signals, we combine ODT-based structural alignment with lexical alignment and define a progressive reward that measures the improvement from the initial SQL to the final SQL. We further incorporate a progression latency reward that favors earlier correctness and an execution status reward that encourages recovery from the invalid SQL. Experiments on BIRD, Spider, and Spider robustness variants demonstrate that our method consistently improves Text-to-SQL performance across both primary and robustness evaluations.

</details>

*Debjyoti Saha Roy,Byron C. Wallace,Javed A. Aslam*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究推理模型的两阶段机制，可迁移到agent的推理过程设计。

TL;DR: 推理模型在多标签任务中采用“短名单+细粒度推理”的两阶段机制，基于此提出的机制性蒸馏策略优于标准蒸馏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将推理过程分为短名单生成和细粒度推理两个可分离且互补的阶段，并据此设计机制性蒸馏策略。

Conclusion: 推理模型的短名单+细粒度推理机制是可分离且互补的，基于该机制的蒸馏策略能更有效地提升性能。

中文摘要：现代推理模型在具有挑战性的多标签任务中表现出惊人的强零样本性能，这些任务需要从数十万到数百万个候选标签中选择一小部分相关选项。我们研究它们如何从机制上实现这一点。我们将推理描述为一个两阶段过程：先广泛“短名单”候选，然后对结果集进行细粒度推理。我们通过一系列数据集提供证据，表明这些步骤是可分离且互补的。利用这一特征，我们开发了一种机制性蒸馏策略，该策略始终优于标准蒸馏。

Original abstract: Modern reasoning models offer surprisingly strong zero-shot performance on challenging multi-label tasks that require selecting a small set of relevant options from hundreds of thousands to millions of candidate labels. We investigate how they achieve this mechanistically. We characterize reasoning as a two-phase process: A broad "shortlisting" of candidates followed by fine-grained reasoning over the resulting set. We provide evidence across a range of datasets that these steps can be isolated and are complementary. Using this characterization, we develop a mechanistic distillation strategy that consistently outperforms standard distillation.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有TTC扩展策略和评分器碎片化、评估协议不一致，且缺乏对质量-成本权衡的系统分析。

中文摘要：测试时计算（TTC）扩展已成为一种强大的范式，通过在推理过程中分配额外的计算（例如，通过多样本生成和基于验证器的重新排序）来改进大语言模型（LLM）的推理能力。现有的TTC扩展策略和推理评分器仍然碎片化，在不一致的协议下进行评估，并且很少通过质量-成本权衡的视角进行分析。我们介绍了ThinkBooster，一个用于无缝测试时计算扩展LLM推理的统一框架，它包括：(i) 一个模块化的Python库，实现了最先进的TTC扩展策略和评分器系列；(ii) 一个联合评估性能和计算效率的基准测试；(iii) 一个可部署的、兼容OpenAI的代理服务，使得自适应推理能够直接集成到实际应用中。我们还提供了一个演示可视化调试器，用于检查推理轨迹、中间选择决策和替代推理路径。在数学和编码任务上的实证结果揭示了TTC扩展策略和评分方法的性能-计算权衡，并表明ThinkBooster在实际任务中提供了实用的增益。该代码在MIT许可下在线提供。

Original abstract: Test-time compute (TTC) scaling has emerged as a powerful paradigm for improving large language model (LLM) reasoning by allocating additional compute during inference, e.g., via multi-sample generation and verifier-based reranking. Existing TTC scaling strategies and reasoning scorers remain fragmented, evaluated under inconsistent protocols, and are rarely analyzed through the lens of quality-cost trade-offs. We introduce ThinkBooster, a unified framework for seamless test-time compute scaling of LLM reasoning, which consists of (i) a modular Python library implementing state-of-the-art TTC scaling strategy and scorer families, (ii) a benchmark that jointly evaluates performance and computational efficiency, and (iii) a deployable OpenAI-compatible proxy service that enables drop-in integration of adaptive reasoning into real-world applications. We further provide a demo visual debugger for inspecting the reasoning trajectories, intermediate selection decisions, and alternative reasoning paths. Empirical results on mathematical and coding tasks reveal the performance-compute trade-offs of TTC scaling strategies and scoring methods and demonstrate that ThinkBooster provides practical gains in real-world tasks. The code is available online under an MIT license.

### [77] [OpenHalDet: A Unified Benchmark for Hallucination Detection across Diverse Generation Scenarios](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06959v1)

Original abstract: Hallucination detection is essential for the reliable deployment of large language models (LLMs). However, existing evaluations face two core challenges: inconsistent inference configuration and evaluation, and limited coverage of downstream domains and tasks. Consequently, reported detector performance is often difficult to compare, reproduce, and generalize beyond specific experimental settings. We introduce OpenHalDet, a unified benchmark for hallucination detection across diverse generation scenarios. OpenHalDet standardizes the evaluation pipeline, from prompt construction and response generation to truthfulness annotation, detector scoring, and metric computation. It supports heterogeneous detector families under different access settings, including black-box methods that use only generated outputs, gray-box methods that rely on probability-based signals, and white-box methods that exploit internal model signals. By bringing diverse tasks, models, and detectors into a shared framework, OpenHalDet enables controlled comparison and provides a systematic view of how different detection paradigms behave in LLM applications. We release OpenHalDet as an open and extensible codebase to facilitate reproducible evaluation and future development of hallucination detection methods. The code and datasets are available at https://github.com/Nellie179/Hallucination-Detection.

### [78] [TRACE: Trajectory Reasoning through Adaptive Cross-Step Evidence Aggregation for LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07054v1)
*Vijitha Mittapalli,Shreyaa Jayant Dani,Satya Srujana Pilli,Snigdha Ansu,Mohammadreza Teymoorianfard,Franck Dernoncourt,Hongjie Chen,Yu Wang,Ryan A. Rossi,Nesreen K. Ahmed*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM agent轨迹监控框架，可迁移至coding agent安全验证

TL;DR: 提出TRACE框架，通过TIJ循环实现长轨迹恶意行为检测，在SHADE-Arena上F1=0.713，召回率0.844，优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法有效连接长轨迹中时间上分散的证据，难以检测通过一系列良性行为隐藏的恶意目标。

Method: TRACE框架通过TIJ（分诊-检查-判断）循环，先识别高信号区域，再进行针对性检查并跨步骤累积证据，最终输出轨迹级判定。

Result: 在SHADE-Arena十个任务域上，TRACE聚合F1为0.713，召回率为0.844，尤其在需要远距离证据链接的任务上提升最大。

Conclusion: TRACE能有效检测长视野LLM代理的隐藏恶意行为，显著优于现有基线方法。

中文摘要：自主LLM代理可以通过一系列单独良性的行为追求隐藏的恶意目标，使得使用标准轨迹级监控难以检测破坏。现有方法要么在单次传递中评估完整轨迹，要么将它们划分为独立评分的窗口，限制了它们跨时间遥远行为连接证据的能力。我们提出TRACE，一种用于长视野LLM代理轨迹的监控框架。TRACE通过TIJ（分诊-检查-判断）循环操作，识别高信号区域，进行有针对性的检查，同时跨推理步骤维护累积证据，并合成轨迹级判定。我们在SHADE-Arena的十个任务域上评估TRACE，与最先进的基线进行比较。TRACE实现了0.713的聚合F1和0.844的召回率，在需要远距离证据链接的任务上取得了最大的增益。

Original abstract: Autonomous LLM agents can pursue hidden malicious objectives through sequences of individually benign actions, making sabotage difficult to detect using standard trajectory-level monitoring. Existing approaches either evaluate complete trajectories in a single pass or partition them into independently scored windows, limiting their ability to connect evidence across temporally distant actions. We propose TRACE, a monitoring framework for long-horizon LLM agent trajectories. TRACE operates through a TIJ (Triage-Inspect-Judge) loop that identifies high-signal regions, performs targeted inspection while maintaining accumulated evidence across reasoning steps, and synthesizes a trajectory-level verdict. We evaluate TRACE on ten task domains from SHADE-Arena against state-of-the-art baselines. TRACE achieves an aggregate F1 of 0.713 and recall of 0.844, with the largest gains on tasks requiring long-range evidence linking.

### [79] [Less Context, More Accuracy: A Bi-Temporal Memory Engine for LLM Agents Where a Lean Retrieved Context Beats the Full History](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09900v1)
*Liuyin Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出双时间记忆引擎提高LLM agent长程任务准确性，直接可迁移到coding agent。

TL;DR: Engram是一个基于双时间数据模型的开源双过程记忆引擎，通过混合读取路径在LongMemEval_S上以少8倍的token达到83.6%准确率，超过全上下文基线10.4个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代理在跨会话中缺乏长期记忆，现有方法或昂贵缓慢，或准确性低于全上下文基线，且评估标准不一致不可复现。

Method: 提出Engram引擎：双时间数据模型，包含快速写入路径（无LLM追加损失事件）和异步路径（提取原子事实构建知识图并解决矛盾），以及混合读取路径（融合多种信号并应用时间点过滤）。

Result: 在LongMemEval_S上，Engram轻量配置（9.6k token）得分83.6%，全上下文（79k token）得分73.2%，提升了10.4个百分点，且无错误；贡献了可复现的评估工具。

Conclusion: Engram通过双过程设计和混合读取路径有效解决了LLM代理的长期记忆问题，并提供了中立可复现的评估框架。

中文摘要：长期记忆是缺失的LLM代理层：在跨会话中它们会遗忘，而常见的变通方法——将整个历史重放入提示中——既昂贵、缓慢，且随着干扰物的积累，准确性会下降。大多数记忆系统在成本或延迟上获胜，但在准确性上仍落后于全上下文基线，并且基准测试数字是在不一致、不可复现的测试工具上报告的，因此同一系统在不同来源中会出现截然不同的分数。我们提出了Engram，一个基于双时间数据模型的开源双过程记忆引擎。快速写入路径追加无损事件，无需LLM在关键路径上；异步路径提取原子（主语、谓语、宾语）事实，构建双时间知识图，并在无需每个事实调用LLM的情况下解决矛盾——使事实失效，但从不删除，因此每个事实都保留来源和继承链。混合读取路径融合密集、词汇、图以及新近度/显著性信号，应用时间点（“as-of”）过滤器，并组装紧凑的、带有来源标记的上下文。在包含500个问题的完整LongMemEval_S数据集上，由官方类别特定评判器评分，Engram的轻量配置——从约9.6k个token的检索切片中回答，而非整个历史——得分83.6%，而全上下文为73.2%（+10.4个百分点，McNemar检验p < 10^-6），同时token数量减少约8倍（9.6k vs. 79k），且0/500错误。这一增益需要混合读取路径：仅事实会损失召回率，而事实加上检索到的块可恢复细节。我们还贡献了一个中立的、仓库内的评估工具，内置官方评判器，并在每个表格中包含全上下文基线，发布每个问题的原始日志，并记录了无声地扭曲记忆基准测试的测量完整性陷阱（截断、自制的评判器、全历史泄漏）。每个数字都附带可复现它的命令。

Original abstract: Long-term memory is the missing layer for LLM agents: across sessions they forget, and the common workaround -- replaying the whole history into the prompt -- is expensive, slow, and, as distractors accumulate, less accurate. Most memory systems win on cost or latency but still lose to the full-context baseline on accuracy, and benchmark numbers are reported on inconsistent, non-reproducible harnesses, so one system appears at wildly different scores across sources. We present Engram, an open-source, dual-process memory engine on a bi-temporal data model. A fast write path appends lossless episodes with no LLM on the critical path; an asynchronous path extracts atomic (subject, predicate, object) facts, builds a bi-temporal knowledge graph, and resolves contradictions without an LLM call per fact -- invalidating, never deleting, so every fact keeps provenance and a supersession chain. A hybrid read path fuses dense, lexical, graph, and recency/salience signals, applies a point-in-time ("as-of") filter, and assembles a compact, provenance-tagged context. On the full 500-question LongMemEval_S, graded by the official category-specific judge, Engram's lean configuration -- answering from a ~9.6k-token retrieved slice, never the full history -- scores 83.6% vs. 73.2% for full-context (+10.4 points, McNemar p < 10^-6) at ~8x fewer tokens (9.6k vs. 79k), with 0/500 errored. The gain needs a hybrid read path: facts alone lose recall, while facts plus retrieved chunks recover detail. We also contribute a neutral, in-repo evaluation harness with the official judge baked in and the full-context baseline in every table, publish the raw per-question logs, and document the measurement-integrity pitfalls (truncation, home-grown judges, full-history leaks) that silently distort memory benchmarks. Every number ships with a command to reproduce it.

</details>


### [80] [When Large Language Models Fail in Healthcare: Evaluating Sensitivity to Prompt Variations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07237v1)
*Mahdi Alkaeed*

Selection reason: 分析LLM对提示变化的敏感性，方法可迁移到agent提示鲁棒性研究。

TL;DR: 研究表明，即使是对提示进行微小扰动，也会导致医学LLMs产生不一致和危险的输出，尤其是句法重排和对抗性提示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估LLMs在临床应用中面对提示扰动的鲁棒性，因为微小变化可能导致严重风险。

Method: 使用MedMCQA基准，对通用型和医学专用型LLMs进行系统性敏感性分析，将扰动分为自然和对抗类型。

Result: 医学LLMs对简单词汇替换不敏感，但对句法重排和对抗性提示脆弱，可能产生危险输出如错误剂量。

Conclusion: 医学LLMs并非本质安全，在临床应用中不可靠，需要更大的鲁棒性保证。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）在医疗领域的应用日益广泛，例如临床问答、诊断支持和报告摘要。尽管这些模型前景广阔，但它们对微小的提示扰动（包括词汇和句法层面）高度敏感，这在安全关键的临床应用中带来了严重风险。在本研究中，我们使用MedMCQA基准进行系统的敏感性分析，以评估通用型（例如GPT-3.5、Llama3）和医学专用型LLMs（例如ClinicalBERT、BioLlama3、BioBERT）的鲁棒性。我们将扰动分为自然类型和对抗类型，并考察它们对临床推理任务中模型一致性、准确性和可靠性的影响。我们的发现表明，医学LLMs并非本质安全。即使是措辞的微小变化也可能改变临床建议，针对性的对抗性提示可能引发有害输出。在医疗保健等高风险环境中，这种不可预测性是不可接受的——那些因输入措辞改变而更改诊断，或因轻微改写而幻觉药物的模型，无法被临床医生可靠地信任。虽然模型通常对简单的词汇替换或释义表现出韧性，但在句法重排或误导性上下文线索下往往崩溃。这种脆弱性在通用型和领域专用型LLMs中都显而易见。值得注意的是，对抗性操作可能导致临床危险输出，例如推荐错误剂量或遗漏关键发现。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used in healthcare for tasks such as clinical question answering, diagnosis support, and report summarization. Despite their promise, these models remain highly sensitive to subtle prompt perturbations, both lexical and syntactic, posing serious risks in safety-critical clinical applications. In this study, we conduct a systematic sensitivity analysis to evaluate the robustness of both general-purpose (e.g., GPT-3.5, Llama3) and medical-specific LLMs (e.g., ClinicalBERT, BioLlama3, BioBERT) using the MedMCQA benchmark. We categorize perturbations into natural and adversarial types and examine their effect on model consistency, accuracy, and reliability in clinical reasoning tasks. Our findings reveal that medical LLMs are not intrinsically safe. Even minor variations in phrasing can alter clinical advice, and targeted adversarial prompts can provoke harmful outputs. In high-stakes settings like healthcare, such unpredictability is unacceptable-models that change diagnoses due to reworded inputs or hallucinate medications when slightly rephrased cannot be reliably trusted by clinicians. While models tend to show resilience to simple lexical substitutions or paraphrasing, they often break down under syntactic reordering or misleading contextual cues. This fragility is evident across both general-purpose and domain-specific LLMs. Notably, adversarial manipulations can lead to clinically dangerous outputs, such as recommending incorrect dosages or omitting critical findings.

</details>


### [81] [SLMJury: Can Small Language Models Judge as Well as Large Ones?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07810v1)
*Anish Laddha,Nitesh Pradhan,Gaurav Srivastava*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: SLM作为评判者框架，对agent评估有间接启发但非直接agent方法

TL;DR: SLMJury框架评估小语言模型作为裁判，发现快速判定在数学任务中有效，推理在通用任务中更好；不同模型家族在领域泛化和评判能力上存在显著差异；多智能体辩论反而降低准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型作为裁判成本高、延迟大且不透明，需要探索更高效、可解释的小型语言模型作为替代方案。

Method: 提出SLMJury框架，形式化评判为预算条件函数，在16个SLM上测试封闭式和开放式任务，并分析过度思考效应、领域泛化、能力差异及多智能体辩论协议。

Result: 发现过度思考效应具有领域依赖性；领域泛化差距大；封闭式与开放式评判能力不相关；多智能体辩论降低准确率，但顶级裁判对抗攻击稳健。

Conclusion: 可靠自动评估不需要大型专有模型，但无单一小模型占优，需根据任务选择合适模型和策略。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）被广泛用作评估模型输出的裁判，但其高成本、高延迟和不透明性限制了可扩展性。我们引入SLMJury框架，用于评估小型语言模型（SLM）作为裁判的两种范式：封闭式二元正确性和开放式质量评分。我们在十个基准上对来自四个模型家族的16个SLM裁判（0.6B-14B参数）进行基准测试：八个封闭式任务涵盖数学、科学和通用推理（每个配置N=64,824个判断），以及用于摘要和对话评分的SummEval和MT-Bench。我们将评判形式化为预算条件函数，并研究五个维度。四个发现如下：（1）过度思考效应具有领域依赖性：对于大多数裁判，在数学评判中，快速的10个token判定与扩展推理相当或更好（在有助于提升的案例中提高2-7%），而在通用任务中，推理的优势高达23%。（2）领域泛化区分了模型家族，从数学到通用的准确率差距从不到10%到近40%不等。（3）封闭式和开放式评判依赖不同的能力：最佳二元裁判（Phi-4）在MT-Bench上降至第9位，而经过推理训练的模型则逆转了这一顺序。（4）在反思-批评-改进（RCR）辩论协议下，多智能体辩论在所有测试配置中降低了准确率，而顶级裁判在面对六种对抗性角色时方差≤0.55%。可靠的自动评估不需要大型专有模型，但没有单一的SLM占据主导地位。排行榜可在https://anishh15.github.io/SLMJury/ 获取，我们的框架代码和pip包可在https://github.com/anishh15/SLMJury 和https://pypi.org/project/slmjury/ 公开获取。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are widely used as judges for evaluating model outputs, but their high cost, latency, and opacity limit scalability. We introduce SLMJury, a framework for evaluating small language models (SLMs) as judges across two paradigms: closed-ended binary correctness and open-ended quality scoring. We benchmark 16 SLM judges (0.6B-14B parameters) from four model families across ten benchmarks: eight closed-ended tasks spanning mathematical, scientific, and general reasoning (N=64,824 judgments per configuration), plus SummEval and MT-Bench for summarization and conversational scoring. We formalize judging as a budget-conditioned function and study five dimensions. Four findings emerge. (1) The overthinking effect is domain-dependent: for most judges quick 10-token verdicts match or beat extended reasoning on mathematical judging (by 2-7% where they help), while reasoning wins on general tasks by up to 23%. (2) Domain generalization separates model families, with math-to-general accuracy gaps ranging from under 10% to nearly 40%. (3) Closed-ended and open-ended judging draw on different capabilities: the best binary judge (Phi-4) drops to rank 9 on MT-Bench, while reasoning-trained models invert this ordering. (4) Under the Reflect-Critique-Refine (RCR) debate protocol, multi-agent debate degrades accuracy across all tested configurations, whereas the top judges resist six adversarial personas with <=0.55% variance. Reliable automated evaluation does not require large proprietary models, yet no single SLM dominates. The leaderboard is available at https://anishh15.github.io/SLMJury/, and our framework code and pip package are publicly available at https://github.com/anishh15/SLMJury and https://pypi.org/project/slmjury/.

</details>


### [82] [The ACUTE Protocol: Operationalizing Language Model Activations for Better Calibration, Utility, and Trust](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07822v2)
*Nishant Subramani,Palash Goyal,Yiwen Song,Mani Malek,Yuan Xue,Tomas Pfister,Hamid Palangi*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 激活校准与信任估计协议，涉及工具调用任务，可迁移至agent可信度管理

TL;DR: 提出EURO指标和ACUTE协议，平衡校准与信息性，提升LLM的可信赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型校准不良且易被操纵，需要平衡校准和信息性的新方法。

Method: 开发EURO指标和ACUTE协议，后者基于激活值估计置信度、效用和信任。

Result: ACUTE在多项任务和模型上优于强基线，且校准误差低。

Conclusion: ACUTE协议能改进LLM的校准、效用和可信赖性。

中文摘要：随着语言模型的改进并越来越多地被部署到各种任务中，可信赖性变得至关重要。校准是可信赖的一个良好代理：校准良好的置信度估计有助于在信任特定模型输出时权衡风险与回报。不幸的是，即使模型有所改进，它们仍然校准不良，往往偏向于过度自信。此外，校准可能被操纵：一个总是预测基率的策略完美校准，但完全无信息。为了解决这个问题，我们开发了一个新的指标，即通过预言机重新归一化的期望效用（EURO），它平衡了校准和信息性。我们还提出了一种通用的基于激活的置信度、效用和信任估计协议（ACUTE），以适当裁决不确定性。ACUTE协议为3个任务（包括多项选择题回答、工具调用和科学文档摘要）提供了灵活、样本高效和计算高效的置信度估计器，涵盖4个模型家族的6个模型。ACUTE在EURO上优于强基线，同时保持较低的校准误差。综合来看，我们的工作表明，为LLM配备ACUTE协议可以在多种设置下改进校准、效用和可信赖性。

Original abstract: As language models improve and become increasingly deployed to solve a variety of tasks, trustworthiness becomes essential. Calibration is a good proxy for trust: well-calibrated confidence estimates help inform the risk versus reward tradeoff when trusting a specific model output. Unfortunately, even as models improve, they remain poorly calibrated, often biasing towards overconfidence. Additionally, calibration can be gamed: a policy that always predicts the base rate is perfectly calibrated, but completely uninformative. To resolve this, we develop a new metric, expected utility renormalized by the oracle (EURO), that balances calibration and informativeness. We also propose a general-purpose activation-based confidence, utility, and trust estimation protocol (ACUTE) to appropriately adjudicate uncertainty. The ACUTE protocol provides flexible, sample-efficient, and compute-efficient confidence estimators for 3 tasks including multiple choice question answering, tool-calling, and scientific document summarization across 6 models from 4 model families. ACUTE outperforms strong baselines on EURO, while maintaining low calibration error. Taken together, our work shows that equipping LLMs with the ACUTE protocol can improve calibration, utility, and trustworthiness in numerous settings.

</details>

### [83] [TianJi-Environ: An Autonomous AI Scientist for Atmospheric Environmental Research](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07697v1)
*Haoluo Zhao,Hongchun Zhang,Nan Li,Jing-Jia Luo,Kaikai Zhang,Mengyang Yu,Nan Chen,Tao Song,Fan Meng*

Main category: physics.ao-ph

Selection reason: 提出多agent框架用于环境模拟，可迁移到coding agent。

TL;DR: TianJi-Environ是一个基于WRF-Chem的多智能体框架，能够自主驱动大气化学模拟，实现可审计的机制验证。在臭氧和PM2.5案例中，它成功检测了信号并识别了证据不足的环节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大气化学机制验证依赖专家知识和手动实验，缺乏自动化和可审计性。

Method: 构建了首个基于WRF-Chem的多智能体框架，将机制假设自动转化为可执行配置、测试实验和证据标准。

Result: 在臭氧案例中检测到气溶胶-辐射相互作用信号但判断证据不完整；在PM2.5案例中定位了黑碳扰动到颗粒物响应的传播不足和垂直吸收加热诊断缺失。

Conclusion: TianJi-Environ使专家驱动的机制验证变得明确、结构化且可审计，为多智能体系统与复杂大气化学模型耦合提供了可复现范式。

中文摘要：随着大气环境预报的不断改进，污染机制和反馈过程的可解释验证已成为大气化学的主要挑战。然而，基于复杂数值模型的机制验证仍然严重依赖专家知识：机制假设必须转化为可执行的实验，模型输出必须组织成可追溯的证据。我们提出了TianJi-Environ，一种用于大气化学机制验证的可审计AI科学家。TianJi-Environ建立了首个基于WRF-Chem的多智能体框架，能够自主驱动复杂的大气化学模拟，将机制假设转化为可执行的配置、测试实验和证据标准。以臭氧响应和颗粒物反馈作为两个代表性例子，我们展示了TianJi-Environ在机制验证方面的能力。在华北平原夏季臭氧案例中，系统检测到短波辐射和边界层高度中方向一致的气溶胶-辐射相互作用信号，但判断臭氧对NOx控制的响应证据不完整。在关中盆地冬季PM2.5案例中，系统将不支持的联系定位为从黑碳扰动到颗粒物响应的传播不足以及垂直吸收加热诊断的缺失。这些结果表明，TianJi-Environ使专家驱动的机制验证变得明确、结构化且可审计，为与复杂大气化学模型耦合的多智能体系统提供了可复现的范例。

Original abstract: As atmospheric environmental prediction continues to improve, interpretable validation of pollution mechanisms and feedback processes has become a main challenge in atmospheric chemistry. Yet mechanism validation based on complex numerical models still relies heavily on expert knowledge: mechanistic hypotheses must be operationalized into executable experiments, and model outputs must be organized into traceable evidence. We present TianJi-Environ, an auditable AI Scientist for atmospheric-chemistry mechanism validation. TianJi-Environ establishes the first WRF-Chem-based multi-agent framework that autonomously drives complex atmospheric-chemistry simulations, converting mechanistic hypotheses into executable configurations, testing experiments, and evidence criteria. Using ozone response and particulate-matter feedback as two representative examples, we demonstrate TianJi-Environ's capability for mechanism validation. In a summertime ozone case over the North China Plain, the system detects directionally consistent aerosol-radiation-interaction signals in shortwave radiation and boundary-layer height, but judges the evidence for ozone response to NOx control to be incomplete. In a wintertime PM2.5 case over the Guanzhong Basin, it localizes the unsupported link to insufficient propagation from black-carbon perturbation to particulate response and missing diagnostics of vertical absorptive heating. These results show that TianJi-Environ makes expert-driven mechanism validation explicit, structured, and auditable, offering a reproducible paradigm for multi-agent systems coupled with complex atmospheric-chemistry models.

### [84] [Does Persona Make LLMs K-pop Fans? A Pilot Study of LLM-Based Online Concert Audience Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07837v1)
*Kirak Kim,Hyojin Kim,Yejin Son,Sungyoung Kim,Kyung Myun Lee*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: 多agent观众系统，涉及人格与群体行为，但对coding agent直接价值有限

TL;DR: 通过基于人格的LLM多智能体模拟K-pop演唱会粉丝聊天，发现人格条件能提升聊天质量和自然度，但未增强社交连接、参与度或情感反应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究基于人格的LLM观众智能体能否通过实时粉丝聊天重建演唱会集体体验的某些方面。

Method: 构建一个包含十个LLM智能体的多智能体系统，每个智能体以实时聊天消息响应K-pop表演视频，比较人格条件（不同粉丝身份、偏好和聊天风格）与无人格基线，通过被试内设计（N=11位K-pop粉丝）评估效果。

Result: 人格条件显著提高了模型级别的聊天质量和感知自然度，但在社交连接、参与度或情感反应方面未发现显著差异。

Conclusion: 人格条件可使LLM观众看起来更自然，但文化意义上深刻的集体体验可能需要人格、群体行为、粉丝身份和用户期望之间更深入的协调。

中文摘要：演唱会是一种集体体验，但录制的表演视频通常是独自观看，剥夺了使演唱会感觉有事件性的共享观众存在感。我们研究基于人格的LLM观众智能体是否可以通过在K-pop表演视频旁生成实时粉丝聊天来重建这种集体体验的某些方面。我们提出了一个多智能体系统，其中十个LLM智能体通过实时聊天消息做出反应，比较了基于人格的观众（每个智能体被分配一个独特的粉丝身份、偏好和聊天风格）与无人格基线。在一项针对K-pop粉丝（N=11）的被试内试点研究中，人格条件显著提高了模型级别的聊天质量和感知自然度，但在社交连接、参与度或情感反应方面没有转化为差异。访谈表明，在线K-pop演唱会聊天可能表现为集体独白而非人际对话，有意义的参与取决于与特定艺术家和粉丝群体的共同认同。人格条件可以使LLM观众看起来更自然，但文化意义上深刻的集体体验可能需要人格、群体行为、粉丝身份和用户期望之间更深入的协调。

Original abstract: A concert is a collective experience, but recorded performance videos are typically watched alone, stripping away the shared audience presence that makes concerts feel eventful. We investigate whether persona-based LLM audience agents can recreate aspects of this collective experience by generating real-time fan chat alongside a K-pop performance video. We present a multi-agent system in which ten LLM agents react through live-chat messages, comparing a persona-conditioned audience (each agent assigned a distinct fan identity, bias, and chat style) with a no-persona baseline. In a within-subjects pilot with K-pop fans (N=11), persona conditioning substantially improved model-level chat quality and perceived naturalness, but did not translate into differences in social connectedness, engagement, or affective response. Interviews suggest that online K-pop concert chat may operate as collective monologue rather than interpersonal dialogue, and that meaningful participation depends on shared identification with the specific artist and fandom. Persona conditioning can make LLM audiences appear more natural, but culturally meaningful collective experience may require deeper alignment between persona, crowd behavior, fandom identity, and user expectations.

### [85] [Agentic multi-fidelity learning of quasiparticle and excitonic properties](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07836v1)
*Arnab Neogi,Aaron Forde,Christopher A. Lane,Sergei Tretiak,Jian-Xin Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

Selection reason: agent引导的多保真学习框架，通用agent架构可迁移至其他领域

TL;DR: 提出一种智能体引导的多保真度框架，通过诊断GW-BSE计算中的数值脆弱性并应用机器学习修正，有效改善了应变MoS2-WS2双层的激发态计算，显著提高了与高保真度参考的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GW-BSE计算虽准确但计算量大且存在数值不稳定性和收敛失败，在高通量工作流程中难以检测，需要一种自动化的方法来诊断和修正这些问题。

Method: 引入结构智能体，通过分配置信权重和选择性使用少量高精度参考点来评估计算；利用机器学习模型在相关系统间传递信息，并应用高斯过程修正以恢复准粒子隙和激子结合能。

Result: 该方法成功修正了数值诱导的伪影，保留了物理应变依赖性，相比无智能体基线显著提高了与高保真度参考的一致性。

Conclusion: 可靠的激发态代理学习需要明确诊断数值脆弱性，而非直接插值原始数据点；该框架可迁移至其他强量子限域的光电纳米材料。

中文摘要：多体GW-Bethe-Salpeter方程计算对于现代低维纳米材料中电子结构和光学性质的准确模拟至关重要。然而，这些方法计算量大，并且可能表现出局部数值不稳定性或收敛失败，在高通量工作流程中难以检测。我们引入了一种智能体引导的多保真度框架，用于修正应变MoS2-WS2双层中的GW-Bethe-Salpeter激发态景观。在不同堆叠方式、应变分支和倒空间采样下，该工作流程识别出与脆弱的长波介电屏蔽相关的尖峰状偏移、近零带隙崩溃和交叉保真度不一致性。一个结构智能体通过分配置信权重并选择性地使用少量高精度参考点来评估计算。然后，机器学习模型在相关系统间传递信息，并应用高斯过程修正以恢复改进的准粒子隙和激子结合能，同时提供校准的不确定性估计。该方法在不消除物理应变依赖性的情况下修正了数值诱导的伪影，并且相对于无智能体基线显著提高了与高保真度参考的一致性。这些结果表明，可靠的激发态代理学习需要明确诊断数值脆弱性，而不是直接插值原始第一性原理数据点。所提出的框架易于迁移到其他具有强量子限域的 optoelectronic 纳米材料，例如量子点、纳米带、层状二维半导体和杂化钙钛矿纳米结构。

Original abstract: Many-body GW-Bethe-Salpeter equation calculations are essential for accurate simulations of electronic structure and optical properties in modern low-dimensional nanomaterials. However, these methods are computationally demanding and can exhibit localized numerical instabilities or convergence failures that are difficult to detect within high-throughput workflows. We introduce an agent-guided multi-fidelity framework for correcting GW-Bethe-Salpeter excited-state landscapes in strained MoS2-WS2 bilayers. Across stacking registries, strain branches and reciprocal-space samplings, the workflow identifies spike-like excursions, near-zero-gap collapse and cross-fidelity inconsistencies associated with fragile long-wavelength dielectric screening. A structural agent evaluates calculations by assigning confidence weights and selectively using a small number of high-accuracy reference points. Machine learning models then transfer information across related systems and apply Gaussian process corrections to recover improved quasiparticle gaps and exciton binding energies, with calibrated uncertainty estimates. The approach corrects numerically induced artifacts without erasing physical strain dependence and substantially improves agreement with higher-fidelity references relative to a no-agent baseline. These results show that reliable surrogate learning for excited-state materials requires explicit diagnosis of numerical fragility, not direct interpolation of raw first-principles data points. The proposed framework is readily transferable to other optoelectronic nanomaterials characterized by strong quantum confinement, such as quantum dots, nanoribbons, layered two-dimensional semiconductors, and hybrid perovskite nanostructures.

</details>


<div id='cs.MA'></div>

# cs.MA [[Back]](#toc)

### [86] [Hierarchical Certified Semantic Commitment for Byzantine-Resilient LLM-Agent Collaboration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07316v1)
*Haoran Xu,Lei Zhang,Iadh Ounis,Xianbin Wang*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: LLM agent协作中的拜占庭容错协议，提出层次化提交机制，可应用于多agent代码优化场景。

TL;DR: 提出分层认证语义承诺（H-CSC），一种受BFT启发的协议，为LLM智能体协作提供类型化最终性，包括语义提交、判定提交或显式中止，实验表明其有效性和安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决LLM智能体拜占庭协作中朴素聚合隐藏判决细节、经典BFT要求字节同一性不适用的问题，需要一种能输出类型化最终性的协议。

Method: H-CSC协议：根据嵌入导出最终性信号，将提案组划分为三种类型化结果——语义提交（语义核心支持）、判定提交（仅判决级证书）或带原因的中止。

Result: 在BCS_v1上，BFT可行桶提交角度偏差0.31-2.04°，非BFT轮100%中止；在MVR-50上，提交率0.90/0.92，无效率0.02/0.00，语义提交摘要占比74%/72%，消融实验显示判决级回退提升覆盖+0.36/+0.44且安全底线≤0.04。

Conclusion: H-CSC实现了类型化最终性，在保持安全性的同时提升提交覆盖率和可解释性，优于纯语义或纯判决基线。

中文摘要：大型语言模型智能体之间的拜占庭协作需要一种最终性控制原语：给定传递的随机、结构化自然语言提案，协议必须决定该轮是否支持提交、何种类型的提交，或带有类型的安全中止。朴素聚合将这一选择隐藏在单一判定背后；经典拜占庭容错将其隐藏在字节同一性背后，而LLM提案不满足字节同一性。我们引入了分层认证语义承诺（H-CSC），这是一种受BFT启发的协议，它将基于判定条件化提案组的嵌入导出最终性信号转换为三种类型化结果之一：语义提交（指2f+1规模内判定语义核心支持该判定，发出量化聚合上的参数限定摘要），判定提交（较强的判定余量但分散的语义理由，发出判定级证书而不声称语义聚合），或带有类型化原因的显式中止。其贡献在于类型化最终性，而非原始提交准确率。在受控语义投毒诊断测试（BCS_v1，120轮次）中，H-CSC在BFT可行的桶上以低角度偏差（0.31至2.04度）提交，并在超出BFT能力（n<3f+1）的轮次中按预期100%中止。在真实的LLM智能体声明验证基准（MVR-50，50个任务）上，面对成对的静态与急速拜占庭攻击，H-CSC以0.02/0.00的诚实参考无效率分别提交0.90/0.92，与一个强大的发出证书的仅判定基线统计匹配。与基线不同，H-CSC还在74%/72%的轮次上发出基于嵌入的语义提交摘要，提供类型化溯源。严格语义消融仅提交0.54/0.48，表明判定级回退对于覆盖是必要的（+0.36/+0.44），同时保持<=0.04的安全底线；在四个LLM上进行的100任务跨模型检查将无效多数保持在0.00至0.03之间。

Original abstract: Byzantine collaboration among large-language-model agents requires a finality-control primitive: given delivered stochastic, structured natural-language proposals, the protocol must decide whether the round supports a commit, what kind of commit, or a typed safe abort. Naive aggregation hides this choice behind a single verdict; classical Byzantine fault tolerance hides it behind byte-identity that LLM proposals do not satisfy. We introduce Hierarchical Certified Semantic Commitment (H-CSC), a BFT-inspired protocol that converts embedding-derived finality signals over verdict-conditioned proposal groups into one of three typed outcomes: a semantic_commit (a 2f+1 within-verdict semantic core backs the verdict, emitting a parameter-bound digest over the quantised aggregate), a verdict_commit (strong verdict margin but dispersed semantic rationale, emitting a verdict-level certificate without claiming a semantic aggregate), or an explicit abort with a typed reason. The contribution is typed finality, not raw commit accuracy. On a controlled semantic-poisoning diagnostic (BCS_v1, 120 episodes), H-CSC commits with low angular deviation on BFT-feasible buckets (0.31 to 2.04 degrees) and aborts 100% of beyond-BFT rounds (n<3f+1) as intended. On a real LLM-agent claim-verification benchmark (MVR-50, 50 tasks) under paired static and rushing Byzantine attacks, H-CSC commits 0.90/0.92 with honest-reference-invalid rates of 0.02/0.00, statistically matching a strong certificate-emitting verdict-only baseline. Unlike that baseline, H-CSC also emits an embedding-backed semantic_commit digest on 74%/72% of rounds, supplying typed provenance. A strict-semantic ablation commits only 0.54/0.48, showing the verdict-level fallback is necessary for coverage (+0.36/+0.44) at the same <=0.04 safety floor; a 100-task cross-model check across four LLMs preserves invalid_hmaj within 0.00 to 0.03.

</details>

# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [87] [MemDreamer: Decoupling Perception and Reasoning for Long Video Understanding via Hierarchical Graph Memory and Agentic Retrieval Mechanism](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07512v2)
*Cong Chen,Guo Gan,Kaixiang Ji,ZhaoYang Zhang,Zhen Yang,Guangming Yao,Hao Chen,Jingdong Chen,Yi Yuan,Chunhua Shen*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 提出基于agent记忆和检索的视频理解框架，涉及agentic工具使用和层次记忆，可迁移到coding agent。

TL;DR: MemDreamer通过分层图记忆和代理推理循环，将长视频理解的上下文压缩98%并显著提升准确率，取得SOTA结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前VLM处理长视频时因令牌爆炸和注意力稀释而性能受限，需要解耦感知与推理，将长视频理解转化为可扩展的代理探索过程。

Method: 提出即插即用框架MemDreamer，增量流式处理视频构建三层分层图记忆（时空因果基图+语义抽象），推理时通过观察-推理-行动循环进行代理工具增强检索。

Result: 在四个基准上达到SOTA，与人类专家差距仅3.7分；推理上下文窗口仅2%，准确率提升12.5点；发现逻辑推理与长视频理解性能强正相关。

Conclusion: 代理能力扩展成为多模态理解的新范式，证明通过结构化记忆和代理推理可有效突破长视频理解瓶颈。

中文摘要：当前视觉语言模型在处理数小时长的视频时面临困难，因为处理全长度视觉序列会导致令牌爆炸和注意力稀释。为了解决这个问题，我们引入MemDreamer，将感知和推理解耦，将长视频理解转变为代理探索过程。作为一个即插即用框架，它增量式地流式传输视频以构建分层图记忆，一个自顶向下的三层架构用于语义抽象，由捕获时空和因果关系的基图锚定。在推理时，推理模型采用代理工具增强检索，通过观察-推理-行动循环导航层次结构、搜索节点和遍历逻辑边。实验表明，MemDreamer在四个主流基准上取得最先进结果，将与人类专家的差距缩小到仅3.7个百分点。它将推理上下文窗口限制在全上下文摄入的仅2%，同时提供了12.5个百分点的绝对准确度提升。此外，统计分析发现VLM在逻辑推理和长视频理解基准上的性能之间存在强正线性相关，将代理能力扩展确立为多模态理解的新范式。

Original abstract: Current Vision-Language Models struggle with hours-long videos because processing full-length visual sequences induces prohibitive token explosion and attention dilution. To overcome this, we introduce MemDreamer to decouple perception and reasoning, shifting long-video understanding into an agentic exploration process. As a plug-and-play framework, it incrementally streams videos to construct a Hierarchical Graph Memory, a top-down three-tier architecture for semantic abstraction, anchored by a foundational graph capturing spatiotemporal and causal relations. During inference, the reasoning model employs agentic tool-augmented retrieval, navigating hierarchies, searching nodes, and traversing logical edges via an Observation-Reason-Action loop. Experiments show MemDreamer achieves SOTA results across four mainstream benchmarks, narrowing the gap with human experts to only 3.7 points. It constrains the reasoning context window to merely 2% of full-context ingestion while delivering a 12.5 point absolute accuracy gain. Furthermore, statistical analysis uncovers a strong positive linear correlation between an VLM's performance on logic reasoning and long-video understanding benchmarks, establishing agentic capability scaling as a new paradigm for multimodal comprehension.

</details>


<div id='cs.ET'></div>

# cs.ET [[Back]](#toc)

### [88] [The Three-Ring Architecture: Governing Agents in the Era of On-Platform Organisations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07119v1)
*Sergio Alvarez-Telena,Marta Diez-Fernandez*

Main category: cs.ET

Selection reason: 多环代理治理架构，对agent安全部署有启发

TL;DR: 针对当前企业AI部署缺乏治理导致高失败率的问题，提出三环架构，其中环2作为确定性操作系统管理智能体，环3的LLM引入非确定性风险，治理需随LLM能力提升而增强，该架构已历经十年多行业验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前企业AI部署面临结构性失败：组织获得智能体能力但缺乏治理基础设施，导致类似第一波AI部署的高失败率（95%）。

Method: 形式化定义三环架构：环1（现有生产架构）、环2（基于策略的智能体AI的M2联合层，作为智能体企业的操作系统）、环3（基于LLM的前沿智能层），并区分环2（确定性）与环3（非确定性）的风险特征。

Result: 该架构在金融服务、政府、采购和合规等领域的十年部署中得到验证，表明环2是控制与合规的必要条件，且LLM能力提升是架构的结构性顺风。

Conclusion: 提升LLM能力会放大其非确定性偏差的后果，因此治理需求随能力增长而扩展，三环架构是应对这一挑战的关键基础设施。

中文摘要：当前企业AI部署阶段面临结构性失败：组织在获取智能体能力的同时缺乏治理基础设施。预计这将重蹈第一波AI部署的覆辙：去中心化智能缺乏联合层，导致95%的项目失败率。本文正式提出三环架构作为平台型企业的治理基础设施。环1为现有生产架构；环2为基于策略的智能体AI构建的M2联合层；环3为基于LLM的前沿智能层。环2在技术精确意义上构成了智能体企业的操作系统——在组织层面执行计算操作系统在设备层面所执行的功能：资源抽象、流程协调、权限执行以及一个用于复合智能的稳定平台。核心贡献在于正式区分了环2与环3的风险特征。基于策略的智能体在确定性框架内运行：其后果可追溯，权限可执行，偏差可恢复。基于LLM的智能体则引入了截然不同的风险：非确定性行为者，其偏差通过复杂组织系统传播，且无法进行追溯性回溯。环2并非有益的补充——它是控制与合规的必要条件。进一步的结论：LLM能力的每一次提升都是这一架构的结构性顺风。能力更强的非确定性行为者在发生偏差时会产生更大的后果。治理需求随能力增长而扩展。该架构已在金融服务、政府、采购和合规等多个领域经过十年的部署验证。

Original abstract: The current phase of enterprise AI deployment faces a structural failure: organisations are acquiring agentic capability without the infrastructure to govern it. The result is expected to reproduce the error of the first wave of AI deployment: decentralised intelligence without a federation layer leading to a 95% project failure rate. This paper formalises the Three-Ring Architecture as the governing infrastructure of the on-platform organisation. Ring 1 is the existing production architecture; Ring 2 is the M2 federation layer built on strategies-based agentic AI; Ring 3 is the LLM-based frontier intelligence layer. Ring 2 constitutes, in the technically exact sense, the operating system of the agentic enterprise - performing at the organisational level what a computing OS performs at the device level: resource abstraction, process coordination, permission enforcement, and a stable platform for compounding intelligence. A central contribution is the formal distinction between Ring 2 and Ring 3 risk profiles. Strategies-based agents operate within a deterministic framework: their consequences are traceable, their permissions enforceable, their deviations recoverable. LLM-based agents introduce a categorically distinct risk: a non-deterministic actor whose deviations propagate through complex organisational systems without retrospective traceability. Ring 2 is not a useful addition - it is a necessary condition of control and compliance. A further consequence: every improvement in LLM capability is a structural tailwind for this architecture. More capable non-deterministic actors produce larger consequences when they deviate. The governance requirement scales with capability. The architecture has been validated across a decade of deployment in financial services, government, procurement, and compliance among other sectors.

</details>
